### File 10: gradlew
**Path:** `android\gradlew`
**Size:** 4.85 KB

```text
#!/usr/bin/env bash

##############################################################################
##
##  Gradle start up script for UN*X
##
##############################################################################

# Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=""

APP_NAME="Gradle"
APP_BASE_NAME=`basename "$0"`

# Use the maximum available, or set MAX_FD != -1 to use that value.
MAX_FD="maximum"

warn ( ) {
    echo "$*"
}

die ( ) {
    echo
    echo "$*"
    echo
    exit 1
}

# OS specific support (must be 'true' or 'false').
cygwin=false
msys=false
darwin=false
case "`uname`" in
  CYGWIN* )
    cygwin=true
    ;;
  Darwin* )
    darwin=true
    ;;
  MINGW* )
    msys=true
    ;;
esac

# Attempt to set APP_HOME
# Resolve links: $0 may be a link
PRG="$0"
# Need this for relative symlinks.
while [ -h "$PRG" ] ; do
    ls=`ls -ld "$PRG"`
    link=`expr "$ls" : '.*-> \(.*\)$'`
    if expr "$link" : '/.*' > /dev/null; then
        PRG="$link"
    else
        PRG=`dirname "$PRG"`"/$link"
    fi
done
SAVED="`pwd`"
cd "`dirname \"$PRG\"`/" >/dev/null
APP_HOME="`pwd -P`"
cd "$SAVED" >/dev/null

CLASSPATH=$APP_HOME/gradle/wrapper/gradle-wrapper.jar

# Determine the Java command to use to start the JVM.
if [ -n "$JAVA_HOME" ] ; then
    if [ -x "$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java" ] ; then
        # IBM's JDK on AIX uses strange locations for the executables
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/jre/sh/java"
    else
        JAVACMD="$JAVA_HOME/bin/java"
    fi
    if [ ! -x "$JAVACMD" ] ; then
        die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: $JAVA_HOME

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
    fi
else
    JAVACMD="java"
    which java >/dev/null 2>&1 || die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.

Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
location of your Java installation."
fi

# Increase the maximum file descriptors if we can.
if [ "$cygwin" = "false" -a "$darwin" = "false" ] ; then
    MAX_FD_LIMIT=`ulimit -H -n`
    if [ $? -eq 0 ] ; then
        if [ "$MAX_FD" = "maximum" -o "$MAX_FD" = "max" ] ; then
            MAX_FD="$MAX_FD_LIMIT"
        fi
        ulimit -n $MAX_FD
        if [ $? -ne 0 ] ; then
            warn "Could not set maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD"
        fi
    else
        warn "Could not query maximum file descriptor limit: $MAX_FD_LIMIT"
    fi
fi

# For Darwin, add options to specify how the application appears in the dock
if $darwin; then
    GRADLE_OPTS="$GRADLE_OPTS \"-Xdock:name=$APP_NAME\" \"-Xdock:icon=$APP_HOME/media/gradle.icns\""
fi

# For Cygwin, switch paths to Windows format before running java
if $cygwin ; then
    APP_HOME=`cygpath --path --mixed "$APP_HOME"`
    CLASSPATH=`cygpath --path --mixed "$CLASSPATH"`
    JAVACMD=`cygpath --unix "$JAVACMD"`

    # We build the pattern for arguments to be converted via cygpath
    ROOTDIRSRAW=`find -L / -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d 2>/dev/null`
    SEP=""
    for dir in $ROOTDIRSRAW ; do
        ROOTDIRS="$ROOTDIRS$SEP$dir"
        SEP="|"
    done
    OURCYGPATTERN="(^($ROOTDIRS))"
    # Add a user-defined pattern to the cygpath arguments
    if [ "$GRADLE_CYGPATTERN" != "" ] ; then
        OURCYGPATTERN="$OURCYGPATTERN|($GRADLE_CYGPATTERN)"
    fi
    # Now convert the arguments - kludge to limit ourselves to /bin/sh
    i=0
    for arg in "$@" ; do
        CHECK=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "$OURCYGPATTERN" -`
        CHECK2=`echo "$arg"|egrep -c "^-"`                                 ### Determine if an option

        if [ $CHECK -ne 0 ] && [ $CHECK2 -eq 0 ] ; then                    ### Added a condition
            eval `echo args$i`=`cygpath --path --ignore --mixed "$arg"`
        else
            eval `echo args$i`="\"$arg\""
        fi
        i=$((i+1))
    done
    case $i in
        (0) set -- ;;
        (1) set -- "$args0" ;;
        (2) set -- "$args0" "$args1" ;;
        (3) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" ;;
        (4) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" ;;
        (5) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" ;;
        (6) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" ;;
        (7) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" ;;
        (8) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" ;;
        (9) set -- "$args0" "$args1" "$args2" "$args3" "$args4" "$args5" "$args6" "$args7" "$args8" ;;
    esac
fi

# Split up the JVM_OPTS And GRADLE_OPTS values into an array, following the shell quoting and substitution rules
function splitJvmOpts() {
    JVM_OPTS=("$@")
}
eval splitJvmOpts $DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS $JAVA_OPTS $GRADLE_OPTS
JVM_OPTS[${#JVM_OPTS[*]}]="-Dorg.gradle.appname=$APP_BASE_NAME"

exec "$JAVACMD" "${JVM_OPTS[@]}" -classpath "$CLASSPATH" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain "$@"

```

### File 11: gradlew.bat
**Path:** `android\gradlew.bat`
**Size:** 2.35 KB

```text
@if "%DEBUG%" == "" @echo off
@rem ##########################################################################
@rem
@rem  Gradle startup script for Windows
@rem
@rem ##########################################################################

@rem Set local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" setlocal

@rem Add default JVM options here. You can also use JAVA_OPTS and GRADLE_OPTS to pass JVM options to this script.
set DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS=

set DIRNAME=%~dp0
if "%DIRNAME%" == "" set DIRNAME=.
set APP_BASE_NAME=%~n0
set APP_HOME=%DIRNAME%

@rem Find java.exe
if defined JAVA_HOME goto findJavaFromJavaHome

set JAVA_EXE=java.exe
%JAVA_EXE% -version >NUL 2>&1
if "%ERRORLEVEL%" == "0" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:findJavaFromJavaHome
set JAVA_HOME=%JAVA_HOME:"=%
set JAVA_EXE=%JAVA_HOME%/bin/java.exe

if exist "%JAVA_EXE%" goto init

echo.
echo ERROR: JAVA_HOME is set to an invalid directory: %JAVA_HOME%
echo.
echo Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the
echo location of your Java installation.

goto fail

:init
@rem Get command-line arguments, handling Windowz variants

if not "%OS%" == "Windows_NT" goto win9xME_args
if "%@eval[2+2]" == "4" goto 4NT_args

:win9xME_args
@rem Slurp the command line arguments.
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=
set _SKIP=2

:win9xME_args_slurp
if "x%~1" == "x" goto execute

set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%*
goto execute

:4NT_args
@rem Get arguments from the 4NT Shell from JP Software
set CMD_LINE_ARGS=%$

:execute
@rem Setup the command line

set CLASSPATH=%APP_HOME%\gradle\wrapper\gradle-wrapper.jar

@rem Execute Gradle
"%JAVA_EXE%" %DEFAULT_JVM_OPTS% %JAVA_OPTS% %GRADLE_OPTS% "-Dorg.gradle.appname=%APP_BASE_NAME%" -classpath "%CLASSPATH%" org.gradle.wrapper.GradleWrapperMain %CMD_LINE_ARGS%

:end
@rem End local scope for the variables with windows NT shell
if "%ERRORLEVEL%"=="0" goto mainEnd

:fail
rem Set variable GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE if you need the _script_ return code instead of
rem the _cmd.exe /c_ return code!
if  not "" == "%GRADLE_EXIT_CONSOLE%" exit 1
exit /b 1

:mainEnd
if "%OS%"=="Windows_NT" endlocal

:omega

```

### File 15: GeneratedPluginRegistrant.java

```java
package io.flutter.plugins;

import androidx.annotation.Keep;
import androidx.annotation.NonNull;
import io.flutter.Log;
```

```markdown
# Launch Screen Assets

You can customize the launch screen with your own desired assets by replacing the image files in this directory.

You can also do it by opening your Flutter project's Xcode project with `open ios/Runner.xcworkspace`, selecting `Runner/Assets.xcassets` in the Project Navigator and dropping in the desired images.
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import 'screens/camera/ui/camera_screen.dart';

void main() async {
  WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized();

  // Lock orientation to portrait
  await SystemChrome.setPreferredOrientations([
    DeviceOrientation.portraitUp,
  ]);

  // Set status bar style
  SystemChrome.setSystemUIOverlayStyle(
    const SystemUiOverlayStyle(
      statusBarColor: Colors.transparent,
      statusBarIconBrightness: Brightness.light,
      systemNavigationBarColor: Colors.black,
      systemNavigationBarIconBrightness: Brightness.light,
    ),
  );

  runApp(const MyApp());
}

class MyApp extends StatelessWidget {
  const MyApp({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      title: 'ScanIQ',
      theme: ThemeData(
        colorScheme: ColorScheme.fromSeed(
          seedColor: const Color(0xFFFF6B35),
          brightness: Brightness.dark,
        ),
        useMaterial3: true,
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: Colors.black,
      ),
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      home: const CameraScreen(),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 33: app_routes.dart
**Path:** `lib\core\routes\app_routes.dart`
**Size:** 1.70 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../screens/splash/splash_screen.dart';
import '../../screens/home/home_screen.dart';
import '../../screens/camera/camera_screen_v2.dart'; // âœ… Updated import

/// âœ… App Routes Configuration
class AppRoutes {
  // Route names
  static const String splash = '/';
  static const String home = '/home';
  static const String camera = '/camera';

  /// âœ… All app routes mapping
  static Map<String, WidgetBuilder> get routes {
    return {
      splash: (context) => const SplashScreen(),
      home: (context) => const HomeScreen(),
      camera: (context) => const CameraScreenV2(), // âœ… Using new camera screen
    };
  }

  /// âœ… Navigation helper methods

  /// Navigate to Home (replace current route)
  static void navigateToHome(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.pushReplacementNamed(context, home);
  }

  /// Navigate to Camera (push new route)
  static void navigateToCamera(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.pushNamed(context, camera);
  }

  /// Navigate to Camera with result handling
  static Future<bool?> navigateToCameraWithResult(BuildContext context) async {
    return await Navigator.pushNamed<bool>(context, camera);
  }

  /// Pop back to previous screen
  static void goBack(BuildContext context, [dynamic result]) {
    if (Navigator.canPop(context)) {
      Navigator.pop(context, result);
    }
  }

  /// Pop until home screen
  static void popToHome(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.popUntil(context, (route) => route.settings.name == home);
  }

  /// Pop until root (splash)
  static void popToRoot(BuildContext context) {
    Navigator.popUntil(context, (route) => route.isFirst);
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../constants/app_colors.dart';

class AppTheme {
  static ThemeData get lightTheme {
    return ThemeData(
      useMaterial3: true,
      brightness: Brightness.light,
      primaryColor: AppColors.primary,
      scaffoldBackgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundLight,
      fontFamily: 'Inter',

      colorScheme: const ColorScheme.light(
        primary: AppColors.primary,
        secondary: AppColors.primaryLight,
        surface: AppColors.cardBackground,
        error: AppColors.error,
      ),

      appBarTheme: const AppBarTheme(
        elevation: 0,
        backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
        iconTheme: IconThemeData(color: AppColors.textPrimary),
      ),
    );
  }

  static ThemeData get darkTheme {
    return ThemeData(
      useMaterial3: true,
      brightness: Brightness.dark,
      primaryColor: AppColors.primary,
      scaffoldBackgroundColor: AppColors.backgroundDark,
      fontFamily: 'Inter',

      colorScheme: const ColorScheme.dark(
        primary: AppColors.primary,
        secondary: AppColors.primaryLight,
        surface: Color(0xFF2C2C2C),
        error: AppColors.error,
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
class CameraPresetConfig {
  // âœ… Optimized for performance
  static const int imageWidth = 1920;
  static const int imageHeight = 1080;
  static const int quality = 85;
  static const int maxFrameRate = 30;

  // âœ… Memory management
  static const int cacheWidth = 800;
  static const int cacheHeight = 1200;
  static const bool enableAudio = false;

  // âœ… Detection intervals
  static const Duration detectionInterval = Duration(seconds: 1);
  static const Duration captureDelay = Duration(milliseconds: 200);

  // âœ… Quality thresholds
  static const double minBlurScore = 80.0;
  static const double minBrightness = 0.3;
  static const double maxBrightness = 0.85;
  static const double minConfidence = 0.7;
}

class CameraStateConfig {
  final bool isInitialized;
  final bool isProcessing;
  final bool isCapturing;
  final bool isDetecting;

  const CameraStateConfig({
    this.isInitialized = false,
    this.isProcessing = false,
    this.isCapturing = false,
    this.isDetecting = false,
  });

  CameraStateConfig copyWith({
    bool? isInitialized,
    bool? isProcessing,
    bool? isCapturing,
    bool? isDetecting,
  }) {
    return CameraStateConfig(
      isInitialized: isInitialized ?? this.isInitialized,
      isProcessing: isProcessing ?? this.isProcessing,
      isCapturing: isCapturing ?? this.isCapturing,
      isDetecting: isDetecting ?? this.isDetecting,
    );
  }

  bool get isBusy => isProcessing || isCapturing || isDetecting;
}
```

### File 36: document_model.dart
**Path:** `lib\models\document_model.dart`
**Size:** 835.00 Bytes

```dart
class DocumentModel {
  final String id;
  final String name;
  final String path;
  final DateTime dateCreated;
  final double sizeInMB;
  final DocumentType type;

  DocumentModel({
    required this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.path,
    required this.dateCreated,
    required this.sizeInMB,
    required this.type,
  });

  String get formattedDate {
    final months = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun',
      'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
    return '${months[dateCreated.month - 1]} ${dateCreated.day}, ${dateCreated.year}';
  }

  String get formattedSize {
    if (sizeInMB < 1) {
      return '${(sizeInMB * 1024).toStringAsFixed(0)} KB';
    }
    return '${sizeInMB.toStringAsFixed(1)} MB';
  }
}

enum DocumentType {
  pdf,
  image,
  document,
}

```

### File 37: edit_state.dart
**Path:** `lib\models\edit_state.dart`
**Size:** 1.99 KB

```dart
import 'dart:ui';

/// Document edit state model
class DocumentEditState {
  final String imagePath;
  final DocumentFilter selectedFilter;
  final List<Offset> corners;
  final double rotation;
  final bool isProcessing;
  final bool cornersDetected;

  const DocumentEditState({
    required this.imagePath,
    this.selectedFilter = DocumentFilter.original,
    this.corners = const [],
    this.rotation = 0.0,
    this.isProcessing = false,
    this.cornersDetected = false,
  });

  DocumentEditState copyWith({
    String? imagePath,
    DocumentFilter? selectedFilter,
    List<Offset>? corners,
    double? rotation,
    bool? isProcessing,
    bool? cornersDetected,
  }) {
    return DocumentEditState(
      imagePath: imagePath ?? this.imagePath,
      selectedFilter: selectedFilter ?? this.selectedFilter,
      corners: corners ?? this.corners,
      rotation: rotation ?? this.rotation,
      isProcessing: isProcessing ?? this.isProcessing,
      cornersDetected: cornersDetected ?? this.cornersDetected,
    );
  }
}

/// Available document filters
enum DocumentFilter {
  original,
  blackWhite,
  enhanced,
  grayscale,
  magic;

  String get displayName {
    switch (this) {
      case DocumentFilter.original:
        return 'Original';
      case DocumentFilter.blackWhite:
        return 'B&W';
      case DocumentFilter.enhanced:
        return 'Enhanced';
      case DocumentFilter.grayscale:
        return 'Grayscale';
      case DocumentFilter.magic:
        return 'Magic';
    }
  }

  String get description {
    switch (this) {
      case DocumentFilter.original:
        return 'No filter applied';
      case DocumentFilter.blackWhite:
        return 'High contrast scanner mode';
      case DocumentFilter.enhanced:
        return 'Color boost and clarity';
      case DocumentFilter.grayscale:
        return 'Black and white tones';
      case DocumentFilter.magic:
        return 'AI-powered auto enhance';
    }
  }
}

```

### File 38: scan_state.dart
**Path:** `lib\models\scan_state.dart`

```dart
enum CameraMode { auto, manual }

enum CameraFlashMode { off, on, auto }

enum ScanState {
  idle,
  detecting,
  ready,
  capturing,
  processing,
  blur,
  tilted,
  tooSmall,
}

class CameraConfig {
  final CameraMode mode;
  final CameraFlashMode flashMode;
  final bool gridVisible;
  final int pageCount;
  final ScanState state;
  final bool isDocumentDetected;
  final double detectionConfidence;

  const CameraConfig({
    this.mode = CameraMode.manual, // âœ… FIXED: Manual mode by default
    this.flashMode = CameraFlashMode.off,
    this.gridVisible = false,
    this.pageCount = 0,
    this.state = ScanState.idle,
    this.isDocumentDetected = false,
    this.detectionConfidence = 0.0,
  });

  CameraConfig copyWith({
    CameraMode? mode,
    CameraFlashMode? flashMode,
    bool? gridVisible,
    int? pageCount,
    ScanState? state,
    bool? isDocumentDetected,
    double? detectionConfidence,
  }) {
    return CameraConfig(
      mode: mode ?? this.mode,
      flashMode: flashMode ?? this.flashMode,
      gridVisible: gridVisible ?? this.gridVisible,
      pageCount: pageCount ?? this.pageCount,
      state: state ?? this.state,
      isDocumentDetected: isDocumentDetected ?? this.isDocumentDetected,
      detectionConfidence: detectionConfidence ?? this.detectionConfidence,
    );
  }

  bool get isAutoMode => mode == CameraMode.auto;
  bool get isFlashOn => flashMode == CameraFlashMode.on;
  bool get isFlashAuto => flashMode == CameraFlashMode.auto;

  // âœ… FIXED: Always allow capture in manual mode
  bool get canCapture => true;

  String get modeText => mode == CameraMode.auto ? 'Auto' : 'Manual';

  String get flashModeText {
    switch (flashMode) {
      case CameraFlashMode.on:
        return 'ON';
      case CameraFlashMode.auto:
        return 'AUTO';
      default:
        return 'OFF';
    }
  }

  String get hintText {
    switch (state) {
      case ScanState.detecting:
        return 'Detecting document...';
      case ScanState.ready:
        return isAutoMode ? 'Auto capture in 1 sec' : 'Tap to capture';
      case ScanState.capturing:
        return 'Capturing...';
      case ScanState.processing:
        return 'Processing...';
      case ScanState.blur:
        return 'Hold steady - Image is blurry';
      case ScanState.tilted:
        return 'Straighten the document';
      case ScanState.tooSmall:
        return 'Move closer to document';
      default:
        return 'Align document within frame';
    }
  }

  bool get shouldShowGreenBorder =>
      isDocumentDetected && state == ScanState.ready && detectionConfidence > 0.8;
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
```

```dart
/// âœ… UI Building Functions (Separated from State)

/// Loading screen widget
Widget buildLoadingScreen() {
  return const Center(
    child: CircularProgressIndicator(
      color: Color(0xFFFF6B35),
    ),
  );
}

/// Main camera view
Widget buildCameraView({
  required BuildContext context,
  required CameraController controller,
  required String? warning,
  required int pageCount,
  required bool isBusy,
  required VoidCallback onCapture,
}) {
  return Stack(
    fit: StackFit.expand,
    children: [
      // âœ… Full screen camera preview
      CameraPreviewFullScreen(
        controller: controller,
        overlay: DetectionOverlay(message: warning),
      ),

      // Top bar (simplified - no config needed for V2)
      _buildTopBar(context),

      // Bottom controls
      _buildBottomControls(
        canCapture: !isBusy,
        onCapture: onCapture,
      ),

      // Page counter
      if (pageCount > 0)
        _buildPageCounter(pageCount),
    ],
  );
}

/// Top bar widget (simplified)
Widget _buildTopBar(BuildContext context) {
  return Positioned(
    top: 0,
    left: 0,
    right: 0,
    child: Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.7),
            Colors.transparent,
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            // Close button
            GestureDetector(
              onTap: () => Navigator.pop(context),
              child: Container(
                width: 44,
                height: 44,
                decoration: BoxDecoration(
                  color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1),
                  shape: BoxShape.circle,
                ),
                child: const Icon(
                  Icons.close,
                  color: Colors.white,
                  size: 24,
                ),
              ),
            ),

            // Title
            const Text(
              'Scan Document',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 18,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),

            // Placeholder for symmetry
            const SizedBox(width: 44, height: 44),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    ),
  );
}

/// Bottom controls widget (simplified)
Widget _buildBottomControls({
  required bool canCapture,
  required VoidCallback onCapture,
}) {
  return Positioned(
    bottom: 0,
    left: 0,
    right: 0,
    child: Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 16),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.transparent,
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.8),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Center(
          child: _buildCaptureButton(
            canCapture: canCapture,
            onCapture: onCapture,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    ),
  );
}

/// Capture button
Widget _buildCaptureButton({
  required bool canCapture,
  required VoidCallback onCapture,
}) {
  final buttonColor = canCapture
      ? Colors.white
      : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.5);
  final borderColor = canCapture
      ? const Color(0xFFFF6B35)
      : Colors.grey;

  return GestureDetector(
    onTap: canCapture ? onCapture : null,
    child: Container(
      width: 72,
      height: 72,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: buttonColor,
        shape: BoxShape.circle,
        border: Border.all(color: borderColor, width: 6),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: borderColor.withOpacity(0.5),
            blurRadius: 20,
            offset: const Offset(0, 4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Icon(
        Icons.photo_camera,
        color: borderColor,
        size: 32,
      ),
    ),
  );
}

/// Page counter widget
Widget _buildPageCounter(int pageCount) {
  return Positioned(
    bottom: 120,
    right: 20,
    child: Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
        horizontal: 12,
        vertical: 8,
      ),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
      ),
      child: Text(
        '$pageCount pages',
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: Colors.white,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
        ),
      ),
    ),
  );
}
```

```dart
/// Preview screen after capturing photo
class CapturePreviewScreen extends StatelessWidget {

    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.pageNumber,

        children: [

              fit: BoxFit.contain,
            ),
          ),

            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            child: _buildTopBar(context),
          ),

          // Bottom controls
          Positioned(
            bottom: 0,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            child: _buildBottomControls(context),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTopBar(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.7),
            Colors.transparent,
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            IconButton(
              icon: const Icon(Icons.close, color: Colors.white, size: 28),
              onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
            ),
            Text(
              'Page $pageNumber',
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 18,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 48),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBottomControls(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.transparent,
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.8),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
          children: [
            // Retake button
            _buildActionButton(
              icon: Icons.refresh,
              label: 'Retake',
              onTap: () {
                HapticFeedback.mediumImpact();
                Navigator.pop(context, false);
              },
            ),

            // Use this photo button
            _buildActionButton(
              icon: Icons.check_circle,
              label: 'Use Photo',
              onTap: () async {
                HapticFeedback.heavyImpact();

                // Navigate to Document Edit Screen
                final result = await Navigator.push<bool>(
                  context,
                  MaterialPageRoute(
                    builder: (_) => DocumentEditScreen(
                      imagePath: imagePath,
                      pageNumber: pageNumber,
                    ),
                  ),
                );

                // Return result to camera screen
                if (context.mounted) {
                  Navigator.pop(context, result ?? true);
                }
              },
              isPrimary: true,
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionButton({
    required IconData icon,
    required String label,
    required VoidCallback onTap,
    bool isPrimary = false,
  }) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 14),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: isPrimary
              ? AppColors.primary
              : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.2),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(
            color: isPrimary ? Colors.white : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.3),
            width: 2,
          ),
          boxShadow: isPrimary
              ? [
            BoxShadow(
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.4),
              blurRadius: 12,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ]
              : null,
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 24),
            const SizedBox(width: 8),
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 16,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'controller/document_edit_controller.dart';
import 'widgets/document_edit_ui.dart';

/// Scan Preview Screen - Main Widget
class DocumentEditScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final int pageNumber;

  const DocumentEditScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.pageNumber,
  });

  @override
  State<DocumentEditScreen> createState() => _DocumentEditScreenState();
}

class _DocumentEditScreenState extends State<DocumentEditScreen> {
  late DocumentEditController controller;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    controller = DocumentEditController(
      imagePath: widget.imagePath,
      pageNumber: widget.pageNumber,
      onStateChange: () => setState(() {}),
    );
    controller.initialize();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return PopScope(
      canPop: !controller.isProcessing,
      onPopInvokedWithResult: (bool didPop, Object? result) {
        if (!didPop && controller.isProcessing) {
          controller.showError('Please wait, processing...');
        }
      },
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.black,
        body: Stack(
          children: [
            DocumentEditUI(
              imagePath: widget.imagePath,
              controller: controller,
              onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
              onShare: controller.handleShare,
            ),
            if (controller.isProcessing || controller.isDetecting)
              _buildOverlay(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOverlay() {
    return Container(
      color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.54),
      child: Center(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            const CircularProgressIndicator(color: Color(0xFFFF6B35)),
            const SizedBox(height: 16),
            Text(
              controller.isDetecting ? 'Detecting document...' : 'Processing...',
              style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontSize: 16),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:io';
import '../../services/edge_detector_service.dart';
import 'document_final_screen.dart';

/// Document Enhancement Screen
class DocumentEnhanceScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final String originalPath;
  final int pageNumber;
  final DocumentDetectionResult detectionResult;

  const DocumentEnhanceScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.originalPath,
    required this.pageNumber,
    required this.detectionResult,
  });

  @override
  State<DocumentEnhanceScreen> createState() => _DocumentEnhanceScreenState();
}

class _DocumentEnhanceScreenState extends State<DocumentEnhanceScreen> {
  String _selectedFilter = 'Original';
  bool _isProcessing = false;

  final List<String> _filters = [
    'Original',
    'Black & White',
    'Grayscale',
    'Enhanced',
    'Sharp',
  ];

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.black,
      appBar: AppBar(
        backgroundColor: Colors.transparent,
        elevation: 0,
        leading: IconButton(
          icon: const Icon(Icons.arrow_back, color: Colors.white),
          onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
        ),
        title: const Text('Enhance Document', style: TextStyle(color: Colors.white)),
      ),
      body: Column(
        children: [
          // Quality badge
          _buildQualityInfo(),

          // Image preview
          Expanded(child: _buildImagePreview()),

          // Filter selector
          _buildFilterSelector(),

          // Bottom controls
          _buildBottomControls(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildQualityInfo() {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: const Color(0xFF23140F),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Icon(
            widget.detectionResult.quality == ScanQuality.excellent ||
                widget.detectionResult.quality == ScanQuality.good
                ? Icons.check_circle
                : Icons.warning_amber,
            color: widget.detectionResult.quality == ScanQuality.excellent ||
                widget.detectionResult.quality == ScanQuality.good
                ? Colors.green
                : Colors.orange,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 12),
          Expanded(
            child: Column(
              crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
              children: [
                Text(
                  'Scan Quality: ${widget.detectionResult.qualityLabel}',
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: Colors.white,
                    fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  ),
                ),
                Text(
                  'Confidence: ${(widget.detectionResult.confidence * 100).toStringAsFixed(0)}%',
                  style: const TextStyle(
                    color: Colors.white70,
                    fontSize: 12,
                  ),
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildImagePreview() {
    return Container(
      margin: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.5),
            blurRadius: 20,
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: ClipRRect(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
        child: Image.file(
          File(widget.imagePath),
          fit: BoxFit.contain,
          cacheWidth: 800,
          cacheHeight: 1200,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFilterSelector() {
    return Container(
      height: 100,
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 12),
      color: const Color(0xFF23140F),
      child: ListView.builder(
        scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
        itemCount: _filters.length,
        itemBuilder: (context, index) {
          final filter = _filters[index];
          final isSelected = _selectedFilter == filter;

          return GestureDetector(
            onTap: () => setState(() => _selectedFilter = filter),
            child: Container(
              width: 80,
              margin: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 12),
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: isSelected ? const Color(0xFFFF6B35) : Colors.grey.shade800,
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              ),
              child: Column(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                children: [
                  Icon(
                    Icons.image,
                    color: Colors.white,
                    size: 28,
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Text(
                    filter,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      color: Colors.white,
                      fontSize: 11,
                    ),
                    textAlign: TextAlign.center,
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBottomControls() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: const BoxDecoration(
        color: Color(0xFF23140F),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(24)),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          children: [
            Expanded(
              child: _buildButton(
                'Retake',
                Icons.camera_alt,
                    () => Navigator.of(context).popUntil((route) => route.isFirst),
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 12),
            Expanded(
              child: _buildButton(
                'Continue',
                Icons.check,
                _handleContinue,
                isPrimary: true,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildButton(String label, IconData icon, VoidCallback onTap, {bool isPrimary = false}) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: _isProcessing ? null : onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 14),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          gradient: isPrimary
              ? const LinearGradient(colors: [Color(0xFFFF6B35), Color(0xFFFF8C61)])
              : null,
          color: isPrimary ? null : Colors.grey.shade800,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 20),
            const SizedBox(width: 8),
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  void _handleContinue() {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(
        builder: (_) => DocumentFinalScreen(
          imagePath: widget.imagePath,
          pageNumber: widget.pageNumber,
          filter: _selectedFilter,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
      BuildContext context,
      String label,
      IconData icon,

                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),

      const SnackBar(content: Text('Document saved successfully!')),
    );
    Navigator.of(context).popUntil((route) => route.isFirst);
```

### File 47: camera_controller.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\controller\camera_controller.dart`
**Size:** 3.87 KB

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';
import '../core/camera_state.dart';
import '../core/camera_lifecycle.dart';
import '../services/camera_initializer.dart';
import '../services/stream_manager.dart';
import '../services/image_capture_service.dart';
import '../detection/auto_capture_logic.dart';

/// Main camera controller - orchestrates all camera operations
class CameraScreenController extends ChangeNotifier {
  CameraState _state = const CameraState();
  CameraController? _camera;

  final _lifecycle = CameraLifecycle();
  final _streamManager = StreamManager();
  late final _captureService = ImageCaptureService(_streamManager);
  final _autoCapture = AutoCaptureLogic();

  // Getters
  CameraState get state => _state;
  CameraController? get camera => _camera;

  /// Initialize camera
  Future<void> initialize() async {
    try {
      debugPrint('ğŸ“¸ Initializing camera...');

      _camera = await CameraInitializer.initialize();
      _lifecycle.attach(_camera!);

      _state = _state.copyWith(isInitialized: true);
      notifyListeners();

      debugPrint('âœ… Camera initialized successfully');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Camera initialization failed: $e');
      _state = _state.copyWith(error: e.toString());
      notifyListeners();
    }
  }

  /// Toggle between auto and manual mode
  void toggleMode() {
    final newMode = !_state.isAutoMode;
    _state = _state.copyWith(isAutoMode: newMode);

    debugPrint('ğŸ”„ Mode changed to: ${newMode ? "AUTO" : "MANUAL"}');

    if (newMode) {
      _startAutoScan();
    } else {
      _stopAutoScan();
    }

    notifyListeners();
  }

  /// Start auto scan mode
  Future<void> _startAutoScan() async {
    if (_camera == null || !_state.isInitialized) return;

    try {
      debugPrint('ğŸ¤– Starting auto scan...');
      _autoCapture.reset();
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Auto scan start failed: $e');
    }
  }

  /// Stop auto scan mode
  Future<void> _stopAutoScan() async {
    if (_camera == null) return;

    try {
      debugPrint('â¹ï¸ Stopping auto scan...');
      await _streamManager.stop(_camera!);
      _autoCapture.reset();
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Auto scan stop failed: $e');
    }
  }

  /// Capture image
  Future<XFile?> capture() async {
    if (_camera == null || !_state.canCapture) {
      debugPrint('âš ï¸ Cannot capture - camera not ready');
      return null;
    }

    debugPrint('ğŸ“· Starting capture...');

    _state = _state.copyWith(isCapturing: true);
    notifyListeners();

    try {
      final image = await _captureService.capture(_camera!);

      if (image != null) {
        debugPrint('âœ… Image captured: ${image.path}');
      } else {
        debugPrint('âŒ Capture failed - no image returned');
      }

      return image;
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Capture error: $e');
      return null;
    } finally {
      _state = _state.copyWith(isCapturing: false);
      notifyListeners();
    }
  }

  /// Pause camera
  Future<void> pause() async {
    debugPrint('â¸ï¸ Pausing camera...');

    await _lifecycle.pause();

    if (_camera != null && _streamManager.isActive) {
      await _streamManager.stop(_camera!);
    }

    _state = _state.copyWith(isPaused: true);
    notifyListeners();
  }

  /// Resume camera
  Future<void> resume() async {
    debugPrint('â–¶ï¸ Resuming camera...');

    await _lifecycle.resume();
    _state = _state.copyWith(isPaused: false);
    notifyListeners();

    if (_state.isAutoMode) {
      await _startAutoScan();
    }
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    debugPrint('ğŸ—‘ï¸ Disposing camera controller...');

    _lifecycle.dispose();
    _streamManager.dispose();
    _autoCapture.dispose();

    super.dispose();
  }
}

```

### File 49: camera_lifecycle.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\core\camera_lifecycle.dart`
**Size:** 1.26 KB

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';

/// Manages camera lifecycle (pause/resume)
class CameraLifecycle {
  CameraController? _controller;
  bool _isPaused = false;

  void attach(CameraController controller) {
    _controller = controller;
  }

  Future<void> pause() async {
    if (_controller == null || _isPaused) return;

    try {
      _isPaused = true;
      debugPrint('ğŸ“¸ Camera paused');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âš ï¸ Pause error: $e');
    }
  }

  Future<void> resume() async {
    if (_controller == null || !_isPaused) return;

    try {
      if (!_controller!.value.isInitialized) {
        debugPrint('âš ï¸ Controller not initialized');
        return;
      }

      _isPaused = false;
      debugPrint('ğŸ“¸ Camera resumed');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âš ï¸ Resume error: $e');
    }
  }

  Future<void> dispose() async {
    if (_controller == null) return;

    try {
      await _controller!.dispose();
      _controller = null;
      debugPrint('ğŸ“¸ Camera disposed');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âš ï¸ Dispose error: $e');
    }
  }

  bool get isPaused => _isPaused;
  bool get isActive => _controller != null && !_isPaused;
}

```

```dart
/// Camera state model
class CameraState {
  final bool isInitialized;
  final bool isCapturing;
  final bool isAutoMode;
  final bool isPaused;
  final String? error;

  const CameraState({
    this.isInitialized = false,
    this.isCapturing = false,
    this.isAutoMode = false,
    this.isPaused = false,
    this.error,
  });

  CameraState copyWith({
    bool? isInitialized,
    bool? isCapturing,
    bool? isAutoMode,
    bool? isPaused,
    String? error,
  }) {
    return CameraState(
      isInitialized: isInitialized ?? this.isInitialized,
      isCapturing: isCapturing ?? this.isCapturing,
      isAutoMode: isAutoMode ?? this.isAutoMode,
      isPaused: isPaused ?? this.isPaused,
      error: error ?? this.error,
    );
  }

  bool get canCapture => isInitialized && !isCapturing && !isPaused;
}
```

### File 51: auto_capture_logic.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\detection\auto_capture_logic.dart`
**Size:** 2.06 KB

```dart
import 'dart:async';
import '../core/camera_config.dart';

/// Auto capture logic with stability check
class AutoCaptureLogic {
  bool _isStable = false;
  Timer? _stabilityTimer;
  int _stableFrameCount = 0;
  bool _hasCaptered = false;

  static const int minStableFrames = 3; // Need 3 consecutive stable frames
  static const int maxStableFrames = 10; // Max frames to wait

  /// Call when document is detected in frame
  void onDocumentDetected() {
    // Don't process if already captured
    if (_hasCaptered) return;

    _stableFrameCount++;

    // Start timer after minimum stable frames
    if (_stableFrameCount >= minStableFrames) {
      _startStabilityTimer();
    }

    // Force capture after max frames (even if timer not done)
    if (_stableFrameCount >= maxStableFrames) {
      _isStable = true;
    }
  }

  /// Call when document is lost or moved
  void onDocumentLost() {
    reset();
  }

  /// Start stability timer (waits for camera to settle)
  void _startStabilityTimer() {
    // Don't restart if already running
    if (_stabilityTimer != null) return;

    _stabilityTimer = Timer(CameraConfig.autoScanDelay, () {
      if (_stableFrameCount >= minStableFrames) {
        _isStable = true;
      }
    });
  }

  /// Reset all state (for retake or document lost)
  void reset() {
    _stabilityTimer?.cancel();
    _stabilityTimer = null;
    _isStable = false;
    _stableFrameCount = 0;
    _hasCaptered = false;
  }

  /// Mark as captured (prevents multiple captures)
  void markCaptured() {
    _hasCaptered = true;
    _isStable = false;
  }

  /// Clean up resources
  void dispose() {
    _stabilityTimer?.cancel();
    _stabilityTimer = null;
  }

  /// Check if ready to capture
  bool get shouldCapture => _isStable && !_hasCaptered;

  /// Check if document is stable
  bool get isStable => _stableFrameCount >= minStableFrames;

  /// Get current stability progress (0.0 to 1.0)
  double get stabilityProgress {
    return (_stableFrameCount / minStableFrames).clamp(0.0, 1.0);
  }
}

```

### File 52: document_validator.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\detection\document_validator.dart`
**Size:** 3.20 KB

```dart
import 'dart:math';

/// Validates if detected region is a valid document
class DocumentValidator {
  static const double minAreaRatio = 0.60; // 60% of screen
  static const double maxAreaRatio = 0.95; // 95% of screen
  static const double minAspectRatio = 0.5; // Min height/width
  static const double maxAspectRatio = 2.0; // Max height/width

  /// Check if detected corners form a valid document
  static bool isValidDocument({
    required List<dynamic>? corners,
    required double screenArea,
  }) {
    // Must have exactly 4 corners
    if (corners == null || corners.length != 4) {
      return false;
    }

    // Calculate area
    final area = _calculateArea(corners);
    final areaRatio = area / screenArea;

    // Check area is within valid range
    if (areaRatio < minAreaRatio || areaRatio > maxAreaRatio) {
      return false;
    }

    // Check if shape is roughly rectangular
    if (!_isRectangular(corners)) {
      return false;
    }

    // Check aspect ratio (not too narrow or wide)
    if (!_hasValidAspectRatio(corners)) {
      return false;
    }

    return true;
  }

  /// Calculate area of quadrilateral
  static double _calculateArea(List<dynamic> corners) {
    // Shoelace formula for polygon area
    if (corners.length != 4) return 0.0;

    try {
      double area = 0.0;
      for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
        final j = (i + 1) % 4;
        final x1 = _getX(corners[i]);
        final y1 = _getY(corners[i]);
        final x2 = _getX(corners[j]);
        final y2 = _getY(corners[j]);
        area += (x1 * y2) - (x2 * y1);
      }
      return (area.abs() / 2.0);
    } catch (e) {
      return 0.0;
    }
  }

  /// Check if corners form a rectangular shape
  static bool _isRectangular(List<dynamic> corners) {
    // Simple check: all angles should be close to 90Â°
    // For now, just check if it's a quadrilateral
    return corners.length == 4;
  }

  /// Check aspect ratio is valid (A4-like documents)
  static bool _hasValidAspectRatio(List<dynamic> corners) {
    try {
      final width = _getDistance(corners[0], corners[1]);
      final height = _getDistance(corners[1], corners[2]);

      if (width == 0 || height == 0) return false;

      final aspectRatio = height / width;
      return aspectRatio >= minAspectRatio && aspectRatio <= maxAspectRatio;
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  /// Get X coordinate from corner point
  static double _getX(dynamic point) {
    if (point is Map) {
      return (point['x'] ?? 0.0).toDouble();
    } else if (point is List && point.length >= 2) {
      return point[0].toDouble();
    }
    return 0.0;
  }

  /// Get Y coordinate from corner point
  static double _getY(dynamic point) {
    if (point is Map) {
      return (point['y'] ?? 0.0).toDouble();
    } else if (point is List && point.length >= 2) {
      return point[1].toDouble();
    }
    return 0.0;
  }

  /// Calculate distance between two points
  static double _getDistance(dynamic p1, dynamic p2) {
    final x1 = _getX(p1);
    final y1 = _getY(p1);
    final x2 = _getX(p2);
    final y2 = _getY(p2);

    return sqrt(pow(x2 - x1, 2) + pow(y2 - y1, 2));
  }
}

```

### File 53: quality_checker.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\detection\quality_checker.dart`
**Size:** 2.79 KB

```dart
/// Checks image quality (blur and brightness)
class QualityChecker {
  // Quality thresholds
  static const int minBlurScore = 75; // 0-100 scale
  static const double minBrightness = 0.3; // 0.0-1.0 scale
  static const double maxBrightness = 0.85;

  /// Check image quality
  static QualityResult check({
    required double blurScore,
    required double brightness,
  }) {
    final issues = <String>[];

    // Check blur
    if (blurScore < minBlurScore) {
      issues.add('Image is blurry');
    }

    // Check brightness
    if (brightness < minBrightness) {
      issues.add('Too dark - add more light');
    } else if (brightness > maxBrightness) {
      issues.add('Too bright - reduce light');
    }

    // Determine overall quality level
    final quality = _getQualityLevel(blurScore, brightness);

    return QualityResult(
      isGood: issues.isEmpty,
      issues: issues,
      blurScore: blurScore,
      brightness: brightness,
      quality: quality,
    );
  }

  /// Determine quality level
  static QualityLevel _getQualityLevel(double blur, double brightness) {
    // Excellent: sharp and well-lit
    if (blur >= 90 && brightness >= 0.4 && brightness <= 0.7) {
      return QualityLevel.excellent;
    }

    // Good: minor issues
    if (blur >= 75 && brightness >= 0.3 && brightness <= 0.85) {
      return QualityLevel.good;
    }

    // Average: noticeable issues
    if (blur >= 60 || (brightness >= 0.25 && brightness <= 0.9)) {
      return QualityLevel.average;
    }

    // Poor: significant issues
    return QualityLevel.poor;
  }
}

/// Image quality levels
enum QualityLevel {
  excellent,
  good,
  average,
  poor,
}

/// Quality check result
class QualityResult {
  final bool isGood;
  final List<String> issues;
  final double blurScore;
  final double brightness;
  final QualityLevel quality;

  QualityResult({
    required this.isGood,
    required this.issues,
    required this.blurScore,
    required this.brightness,
    required this.quality,
  });

  /// Get quality as text
  String get qualityText {
    switch (quality) {
      case QualityLevel.excellent:
        return 'Excellent';
      case QualityLevel.good:
        return 'Good';
      case QualityLevel.average:
        return 'Average';
      case QualityLevel.poor:
        return 'Poor';
    }
  }

  /// Get quality color
  int get qualityColor {
    switch (quality) {
      case QualityLevel.excellent:
      case QualityLevel.good:
        return 0xFF00B894; // Green
      case QualityLevel.average:
        return 0xFFFFB74D; // Orange
      case QualityLevel.poor:
        return 0xFFFF6B35; // Red
    }
  }

  /// Should suggest retake
  bool get shouldSuggestRetake => quality == QualityLevel.poor;
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../controller/document_edit_controller.dart';
import 'widgets/document_edit_ui.dart';

/// Scan Preview Screen - Main Widget
class DocumentEditScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final int pageNumber;

  const DocumentEditScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.pageNumber,
  });

  @override
  State<DocumentEditScreen> createState() => _DocumentEditScreenState();
}

class _DocumentEditScreenState extends State<DocumentEditScreen> {
  late DocumentEditController controller;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    controller = DocumentEditController(
      imagePath: widget.imagePath,
      pageNumber: widget.pageNumber,
      onStateChange: () => setState(() {}),
    );
    controller.initialize();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return PopScope(
      canPop: !controller.isProcessing,
      onPopInvokedWithResult: (didPop, result) {
        if (!didPop && controller.isProcessing) {
          controller.showError('Please wait, processing...');
        }
      },
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.black,
        body: Stack(
          children: [
            DocumentEditUI(
              imagePath: widget.imagePath,
              controller: controller,
              onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
              onShare: controller.handleShare,
            ),
            if (controller.isProcessing || controller.isDetecting)
              _buildOverlay(),
          ],
        ),
      ),

        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,

            ),
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

/// Bottom controls for document edit
class DocumentEditControls extends StatelessWidget {

        boxShadow: [

          ),

      ),

          children: [
            _buildToolbar(),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            _buildActionButtons(context),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildToolbar() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
      children: [
        _buildToolButton(Icons.rotate_right, 'ROTATE', controller.rotateDocument),
        _buildToolButton(Icons.crop, 'CROP', controller.cropDocument),
        _buildToolButton(Icons.tune, 'ADJUST', controller.adjustDocument),
        _buildToolButton(Icons.restart_alt, 'RESET', controller.runDetection),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildToolButton(IconData icon, String label, VoidCallback onTap) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: controller.isProcessing ? null : onTap,
      child: Opacity(
        opacity: controller.isProcessing ? 0.5 : 1.0,
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: const Color(0xFFCE9E8D), size: 24),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(color: Color(0xFFCE9E8D), fontSize: 10),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionButtons(BuildContext context) {
    return Row(
      children: [
        Expanded(child: _buildOutlinedButton('Retake', onBack)),
        const SizedBox(width: 16),
        Expanded(
          child: _buildFilledButton(
            context,
            controller.continueButtonText,
                () => controller.handleContinue(context),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOutlinedButton(String label, VoidCallback onTap) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: controller.isProcessing ? null : onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          border: Border.all(color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35), width: 2),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        ),
        child: Center(
          child: Text(
            label,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: Color(0xFFFF6B35),
              fontSize: 16,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFilledButton(
      BuildContext context,
      String label,
      VoidCallback onTap,
      ) {
    final enabled = controller.canContinue;
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: enabled && !controller.isProcessing ? onTap : null,
      child: Opacity(
        opacity: enabled ? 1.0 : 0.5,
        child: Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            gradient: const LinearGradient(
              colors: [Color(0xFFFF6B35), Color(0xFFFF8C61)],
            ),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          ),
          child: Center(
            child: controller.isProcessing
                ? const SizedBox(
              width: 20,
              height: 20,
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                color: Colors.white,
                strokeWidth: 2,
              ),
            )
                : Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 16,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:io';
import '../../../../services/edge_detector_service.dart';

/// Document preview with detection status
class DocumentPreviewWidget extends StatelessWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final DocumentDetectionResult? detectionResult;
  final bool isDetecting;

  const DocumentPreviewWidget({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.detectionResult,
    required this.isDetecting,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Center(
          child: Container(
            margin: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
              boxShadow: [
                BoxShadow(
                  color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.5),
                  blurRadius: 20,
                  offset: const Offset(0, 10),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            child: ClipRRect(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
              child: Image.file(
                File(imagePath),
                fit: BoxFit.contain,
                cacheWidth: 800,
                cacheHeight: 1200,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
        Positioned(
          top: 16,
          left: 0,
          right: 0,
          child: Center(child: _buildDetectionBanner()),
        ),
        if (detectionResult != null && detectionResult!.detected)
          Positioned(
            top: 60,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            child: Center(child: _buildQualityBadge()),
          ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDetectionBanner() {
    if (isDetecting) {
      return _buildBanner(
        icon: Icons.hourglass_empty,
        label: 'DETECTING...',
        color: const Color(0xFFFFB74D),
      );
    }

    if (detectionResult == null || !detectionResult!.detected) {
      return _buildBanner(
        icon: Icons.warning_amber_rounded,
        label: 'ADJUST DOCUMENT',
        color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35),
      );
    }

    return _buildBanner(
      icon: Icons.check_circle,
      label: 'DOCUMENT DETECTED',
      color: const Color(0xFF00B894),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildQualityBadge() {
    final quality = detectionResult!.quality;
    Color badgeColor;

    switch (quality) {
      case ScanQuality.excellent:
      case ScanQuality.good:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFF00B894);
        break;
      case ScanQuality.average:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFFFFB74D);
        break;
      case ScanQuality.poor:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFFFF6B35);
        break;
    }

    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 6),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: badgeColor.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
      ),
      child: Text(
        'Quality: ${detectionResult!.qualityLabel}',
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: Colors.white,
          fontSize: 11,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBanner({
    required IconData icon,
    required String label,
    required Color color,
  }) {
    return AnimatedContainer(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 8),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: color,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.4),
            blurRadius: 12,
            offset: const Offset(0, 4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 18),
          const SizedBox(width: 8),
          Text(
            label,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white,
              fontSize: 12,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 1.2,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 58: camera_initializer.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\services\camera_initializer.dart`
**Size:** 1.24 KB

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import '../core/camera_config.dart';

/// Single responsibility: Initialize camera ONCE
class CameraInitializer {
  static CameraController? _instance;

  static Future<CameraController> initialize() async {
    if (_instance != null && _instance!.value.isInitialized) {
      return _instance!;
    }

    final cameras = await availableCameras();
    if (cameras.isEmpty) {
      throw Exception('No camera found');
    }

    _instance = CameraController(
      cameras.first,
      CameraConfig.resolution,
      enableAudio: false,
      imageFormatGroup: CameraConfig.format,
    );

    await _instance!.initialize();
    await _setupCamera(_instance!);

    return _instance!;
  }

  static Future<void> _setupCamera(CameraController controller) async {
    try {
      await controller.setExposureMode(ExposureMode.auto);
      await controller.setFocusMode(FocusMode.auto);
      await controller.setFlashMode(FlashMode.off);
    } catch (e) {
      // Ignore setup errors
    }
  }

  static Future<void> dispose() async {
    if (_instance != null) {
      await _instance!.dispose();
      _instance = null;
    }
  }

  static CameraController? get instance => _instance;
}

```

### File 59: image_capture_service.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\services\image_capture_service.dart`
**Size:** 1.09 KB

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import '../core/camera_config.dart';
import 'stream_manager.dart';

/// Single responsibility: Capture image safely
class ImageCaptureService {
  final StreamManager _streamManager;

  ImageCaptureService(this._streamManager);

  Future<XFile?> capture(CameraController controller) async {
    if (!controller.value.isInitialized) {
      return null;
    }

    try {
      // Step 1: Stop stream
      if (_streamManager.isActive) {
        await _streamManager.stop(controller);
      }

      // Step 2: Wait for camera to settle
      await Future.delayed(CameraConfig.captureDelay);

      // Step 3: Verify controller
      if (!controller.value.isInitialized) {
        return null;
      }

      // Step 4: Capture
      final image = await controller.takePicture();

      return image;
    } catch (e) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  Future<void> prepareForRetake(CameraController controller) async {
    // Camera remains initialized, just resume preview
    await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 100));
  }
}

```

### File 60: orientation_handler.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\services\orientation_handler.dart`
**Size:** 1.44 KB

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';

/// Handles device orientation and camera rotation
class OrientationHandler {
  /// Lock device to portrait mode
  static Future<void> lockPortrait() async {
    await SystemChrome.setPreferredOrientations([
      DeviceOrientation.portraitUp,
    ]);
  }

  /// Unlock orientation to all modes
  static Future<void> unlockOrientation() async {
    await SystemChrome.setPreferredOrientations([
      DeviceOrientation.portraitUp,
      DeviceOrientation.portraitDown,
      DeviceOrientation.landscapeLeft,
      DeviceOrientation.landscapeRight,
    ]);
  }

  /// Get camera sensor orientation
  static int getCameraRotation(CameraController controller) {
    return controller.description.sensorOrientation;
  }

  /// Calculate image rotation based on sensor orientation
  static int getImageRotation(int sensorOrientation) {
    // For portrait mode, adjust rotation
    // Most cameras have 90Â° sensor orientation in portrait
    switch (sensorOrientation) {
      case 0:
        return 0;
      case 90:
        return 90;
      case 180:
        return 180;
      case 270:
        return 270;
      default:
        return 0;
    }
  }

  /// Fix image orientation for saving
  static int getFixedRotation(int sensorOrientation) {
    // Return rotation needed to display image correctly
    return (360 - sensorOrientation) % 360;
  }
}

```

### File 61: stream_manager.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\services\stream_manager.dart`
**Size:** 998.00 Bytes

```dart
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import 'dart:async';

/// Manages image stream (start/stop)
class StreamManager {
  bool _isStreaming = false;
  StreamSubscription? _subscription;

  Future<void> start(
      CameraController controller,
      Function(CameraImage) onFrame,
      ) async {
    if (_isStreaming) return;

    try {
      _isStreaming = true;

      await controller.startImageStream((image) {
        if (_isStreaming) {
          onFrame(image);
        }
      });
    } catch (e) {
      _isStreaming = false;
      rethrow;
    }
  }

  Future<void> stop(CameraController controller) async {
    if (!_isStreaming) return;

    try {
      _isStreaming = false;
      await controller.stopImageStream();
    } catch (e) {
      // Ignore stop errors
    }
  }

  Future<void> dispose() async {
    await _subscription?.cancel();
    _subscription = null;
    _isStreaming = false;
  }

  bool get isActive => _isStreaming;
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:provider/provider.dart';
import '../controller/camera_controller.dart';  // âœ… CORRECT PATH
import 'camera_preview.dart';
import 'camera_controls.dart';

class CameraScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const CameraScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<CameraScreen> createState() => _CameraScreenState();
}

class _CameraScreenState extends State<CameraScreen> with WidgetsBindingObserver {
  late final CameraScreenController _controller;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _controller = CameraScreenController();
    _controller.initialize();
    WidgetsBinding.instance.addObserver(this);
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    WidgetsBinding.instance.removeObserver(this);
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  void didChangeAppLifecycleState(AppLifecycleState state) {
    if (state == AppLifecycleState.paused) {
      _controller.pause();
    } else if (state == AppLifecycleState.resumed) {
      _controller.resume();
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return ChangeNotifierProvider.value(
      value: _controller,
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.black,
        body: Consumer<CameraScreenController>(
          builder: (context, controller, child) {
            if (!controller.state.isInitialized) {
              return const Center(
                child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                  color: Color(0xFFFF6B35),
                ),
              );
            }

            return Stack(
              children: [
                const CameraPreviewWidget(),
                const Positioned(
                  bottom: 0,
                  left: 0,
                  right: 0,
                  child: CameraControlsWidget(),
                ),
              ],
            );
          },
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

/// Camera-related dialogs
class CameraDialogs {
  /// Show quality warning before capture
  static Future<bool> showQualityWarning(
      BuildContext context,
      String warning,
      ) async {
    return await showDialog<bool>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text('âš ï¸ Quality Warning'),
        content: Text(warning),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
            child: const Text('Capture Anyway'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    ) ?? false;
  }

  /// Show exit confirmation
  static Future<bool> showExitConfirmation(
      BuildContext context,
      int pageCount,
      ) async {
    if (pageCount == 0) return true;

    return await showDialog<bool>(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text('Discard Scans?'),
        content: Text('You have $pageCount scanned pages. Exit without saving?'),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
            child: const Text('Cancel'),
          ),
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
            child: const Text(
              'Discard',
              style: TextStyle(color: Colors.red),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    ) ?? false;
  }
}
```

### File 66: camera_focus_helper.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\utils\camera_focus_helper.dart`
**Size:** 1.27 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';

/// Helper for camera focus operations
class CameraFocusHelper {
  /// Lock focus for capture
  static Future<void> lockFocusForCapture(CameraController controller) async {
    try {
      final size = controller.value.previewSize!;
      final centerX = size.width / 2;
      final centerY = size.height / 2;

      await controller.setFocusPoint(
        Offset(centerX / size.width, centerY / size.height),
      );

      await controller.setExposurePoint(
        Offset(centerX / size.width, centerY / size.height),
      );

      await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 300));
      debugPrint('âœ… Focus locked for capture');
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Focus lock error: $e');
    }
  }

  /// Manual focus at specific point
  static Future<void> focusAt(
      CameraController controller,
      Offset position,
      Size screenSize,
      ) async {
    try {
      final x = position.dx / screenSize.width;
      final y = position.dy / screenSize.height;

      await controller.setFocusPoint(Offset(x, y));
      await controller.setExposurePoint(Offset(x, y));
    } catch (e) {
      debugPrint('âŒ Manual focus error: $e');
    }
  }
}

```

```dart
/// Camera validation utilities
class CameraValidator {
  /// Check if capture is allowed based on quality
  static bool canCapture({
    required double blur,
    required double brightness,
    bool isAutoMode = false,
  }) {
    if (!isAutoMode) return true;

    return blur >= 80.0 &&
        brightness >= 0.3 &&
        brightness <= 0.85;
  }

  /// Get quality warning message
  static String? getQualityWarning({
    required double blur,
    required double brightness,
  }) {
    if (blur < 60) {
      return 'ğŸ“· Very blurry - Hold steady';
    } else if (blur < 80) {
      return 'ğŸ“· Slightly blurry';
    } else if (brightness < 0.3) {
      return 'ğŸ’¡ Too dark - Turn on flash';
    } else if (brightness > 0.85) {
      return 'â˜€ï¸ Too bright - Reduce glare';
    }
    return null;
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../models/scan_state.dart';

class CameraControls extends StatelessWidget {
  final CameraConfig config;
  final VoidCallback onCapture;
  final VoidCallback onGallery;
  final VoidCallback onGridToggle;
  final bool canCapture; // âœ… NEW: Quality-based capture control

  const CameraControls({
    super.key,
    required this.config,
    required this.onCapture,
    required this.onGallery,
    required this.onGridToggle,
    this.canCapture = true,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 16),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.transparent,
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.8),
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
          children: [
            _buildControlButton(Icons.image, onGallery),
            _buildCaptureButton(),
            _buildControlButton(
              config.gridVisible ? Icons.grid_on : Icons.grid_off,
              onGridToggle,
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildControlButton(IconData icon, VoidCallback onTap) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Container(
        width: 48,
        height: 48,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1)),
        ),
        child: Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 24),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCaptureButton() {
    // âœ… Visual feedback for quality
    final buttonColor = canCapture || !config.isAutoMode
        ? Colors.white
        : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.5);

    final borderColor = canCapture || !config.isAutoMode
        ? AppColors.primary
        : Colors.grey;

    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onCapture,
      child: Container(
        width: 72,
        height: 72,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: buttonColor,
          shape: BoxShape.circle,
          border: Border.all(color: borderColor, width: 6),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: borderColor.withOpacity(0.5),
              blurRadius: 20,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Icon(
          Icons.photo_camera,
          color: borderColor,
          size: 32,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';

/// âœ… Full screen camera preview (no frame, no rounded corners)
class CameraPreviewFullScreen extends StatelessWidget {
  final CameraController controller;
  final Widget? overlay;

  const CameraPreviewFullScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.controller,
    this.overlay,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    if (!controller.value.isInitialized) {
      return const ColoredBox(
        color: Colors.black,
        child: Center(
          child: CircularProgressIndicator(color: Color(0xFFFF6B35)),
        ),
      );
    }

    return Stack(
      fit: StackFit.expand,
      children: [
        // âœ… Full screen preview
        _buildFullScreenPreview(),

        // Overlay (grid, detection borders, etc.)
        if (overlay != null) overlay!,
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFullScreenPreview() {
    final size = controller.value.previewSize!;
    final aspectRatio = size.width / size.height;

    return Center(
      child: AspectRatio(
        aspectRatio: 1 / aspectRatio, // âœ… Portrait mode fix
        child: CameraPreview(controller),
      ),
    );
  }
}

/// âœ… Detection overlay widget
class DetectionOverlay extends StatelessWidget {
  final bool isDetecting;
  final String? message;

  const DetectionOverlay({
    super.key,
    this.isDetecting = false,
    this.message,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    if (message == null && !isDetecting) return const SizedBox.shrink();

    return Positioned(
      top: 100,
      left: 20,
      right: 20,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.7),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
        ),
        child: Text(
          message ?? 'Detecting...',
          style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white),
          textAlign: TextAlign.center,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```
