### File 70: camera_ui_builder.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\widgets\camera_ui_builder.dart`
**Size:** 3.53 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import '../../../models/scan_state.dart';
import '../../camera/widgets/top_bar.dart';
import '../../camera/widgets/camera_controls.dart';
import '../../camera/widgets/quality_indicator.dart';
import '../controllers/camera_event_handlers.dart';

/// Builds camera UI components
class CameraUIBuilder {
  final CameraController? Function() getController;
  final CameraConfig Function() getConfig;
  final double Function() getBlur;
  final double Function() getBrightness;
  final String? Function() getWarning;
  final CameraEventHandlers eventHandlers;

  CameraUIBuilder({
    required this.getController,
    required this.getConfig,
    required this.getBlur,
    required this.getBrightness,
    required this.getWarning,
    required this.eventHandlers,
  });

  /// Build main scaffold
  Widget build(BuildContext context, bool isInitialized) {
    if (!isInitialized || getController() == null) {
      return _buildLoadingScreen();
    }

    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.black,
      body: Stack(
        fit: StackFit.expand,
        children: [
          _buildCameraPreview(),
          _buildTopBar(context),
          _buildQualityIndicator(),
          _buildBottomControls(context),
          _buildPageCounter(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildLoadingScreen() {
    return const Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: Colors.black,
      body: Center(
        child: CircularProgressIndicator(color: Color(0xFFFF6B35)),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCameraPreview() {
    final controller = getController()!;
    return SizedBox.expand(
      child: FittedBox(
        fit: BoxFit.cover,
        child: SizedBox(
          width: controller.value.previewSize!.height,
          height: controller.value.previewSize!.width,
          child: CameraPreview(controller),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildTopBar(BuildContext context) {
    return Positioned(
      top: 0,
      left: 0,
      right: 0,
      child: CameraTopBar(
        config: getConfig(),
        onClose: () => Navigator.pop(context),
        onModeToggle: eventHandlers.toggleMode,
        onFlashToggle: eventHandlers.toggleFlash,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildQualityIndicator() {
    return Positioned(
      top: 100,
      left: 0,
      right: 0,
      child: QualityIndicator(
        blur: getBlur(),
        brightness: getBrightness(),
        warning: getWarning(),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBottomControls(BuildContext context) {
    return Positioned(
      bottom: 0,
      left: 0,
      right: 0,
      child: CameraControls(
        config: getConfig(),
        onCapture: () => eventHandlers.captureImage(context),
        onGallery: () {},
        onGridToggle: eventHandlers.toggleGrid,
        canCapture: true,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildPageCounter() {
    final config = getConfig();
    if (config.pageCount == 0) return const SizedBox.shrink();

    return Positioned(
      bottom: 110,
      right: 20,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 8),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
        ),
        child: Text(
          '${config.pageCount} pages',
          style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../controllers/document_edit_controller.dart';

/// Bottom controls for document edit
class DocumentEditControls extends StatelessWidget {
  final DocumentEditController controller;
  final VoidCallback onBack;

  const DocumentEditControls({
    super.key,
    required this.controller,
    required this.onBack,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
      decoration: const BoxDecoration(
        color: Color(0xFF23140F),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(24)),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: Colors.black26,
            blurRadius: 20,
            offset: Offset(0, -4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            _buildToolbar(),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            _buildActionButtons(context),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildToolbar() {
    return Row(
      mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceAround,
      children: [
        _buildToolButton(
          Icons.rotate_right,
          'ROTATE',
          controller.rotateDocument,
        ),
        _buildToolButton(
          Icons.crop,
          'CROP',
          controller.cropDocument,
        ),
        _buildToolButton(
          Icons.tune,
          'ADJUST',
          controller.adjustDocument,
        ),
        _buildToolButton(
          Icons.restart_alt,
          'RESET',
          controller.runDetection,
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildToolButton(IconData icon, String label, VoidCallback onTap) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: controller.isProcessing ? null : onTap,
      child: Opacity(
        opacity: controller.isProcessing ? 0.5 : 1.0,
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: const Color(0xFFCE9E8D), size: 24),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Color(0xFFCE9E8D),
                fontSize: 10,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionButtons(BuildContext context) {
    return Row(
      children: [
        Expanded(
          child: _buildOutlinedButton('Retake', onBack),
        ),
        const SizedBox(width: 16),
        Expanded(
          child: _buildFilledButton(
            context,
            'Continue',
                () => controller.handleContinue(context),
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOutlinedButton(String label, VoidCallback onTap) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: controller.isProcessing ? null : onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          border: Border.all(color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35), width: 2),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
        ),
        child: Center(
          child: Text(
            label,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: Color(0xFFFF6B35),
              fontSize: 16,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFilledButton(BuildContext context, String label, VoidCallback onTap) {
    final enabled = controller.canContinue;

    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: enabled && !controller.isProcessing ? onTap : null,
      child: Opacity(
        opacity: enabled ? 1.0 : 0.5,
        child: Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            gradient: const LinearGradient(
              colors: [Color(0xFFFF6B35), Color(0xFFFF8C61)],
            ),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          ),
          child: Center(
            child: controller.isProcessing
                ? const SizedBox(
              width: 20,
              height: 20,
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                color: Colors.white,
                strokeWidth: 2,
              ),
            )
                : Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 16,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:io';
import '../../../services/edge_detector_service.dart';

/// Document preview with detection status
class DocumentPreviewWidget extends StatelessWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final DocumentDetectionResult? detectionResult;
  final bool isDetecting;

  const DocumentPreviewWidget({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.detectionResult,
    required this.isDetecting,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Center(
          child: Container(
            margin: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
              boxShadow: [
                BoxShadow(
                  color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.5), // âœ… FIXED
                  blurRadius: 20,
                  offset: const Offset(0, 10),
                ),
              ],
            ),
            child: ClipRRect(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
              child: Image.file(
                File(imagePath),
                fit: BoxFit.contain,
                cacheWidth: 800,
                cacheHeight: 1200,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
        Positioned(
          top: 16,
          left: 0,
          right: 0,
          child: Center(child: _buildDetectionBanner()),
        ),
        if (detectionResult != null && detectionResult!.detected)
          Positioned(
            top: 60,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            child: Center(child: _buildQualityBadge()),
          ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildDetectionBanner() {
    if (isDetecting) {
      return _buildBanner(
        icon: Icons.hourglass_empty,
        label: 'DETECTING...',
        color: const Color(0xFFFFB74D),
      );
    }

    if (detectionResult == null || !detectionResult!.detected) {
      return _buildBanner(
        icon: Icons.warning_amber_rounded,
        label: 'ADJUST DOCUMENT',
        color: const Color(0xFFFF6B35),
      );
    }

    return _buildBanner(
      icon: Icons.check_circle,
      label: 'DOCUMENT DETECTED',
      color: const Color(0xFF00B894),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildQualityBadge() {
    final quality = detectionResult!.quality;
    Color badgeColor;

    switch (quality) {
      case ScanQuality.excellent:
      case ScanQuality.good:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFF00B894);
        break;
      case ScanQuality.average:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFFFFB74D);
        break;
      case ScanQuality.poor:
        badgeColor = const Color(0xFFFF6B35);
        break;
    }

    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 6),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: badgeColor.withValues(alpha: 0.9), // âœ… FIXED
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
      ),
      child: Text(
        'Quality: ${detectionResult!.qualityLabel}',
        style: const TextStyle(
          color: Colors.white,
          fontSize: 11,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBanner({
    required IconData icon,
    required String label,
    required Color color,
  }) {
    return AnimatedContainer(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 8),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: color,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: color.withValues(alpha: 0.4), // âœ… FIXED
            blurRadius: 12,
            offset: const Offset(0, 4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          Icon(icon, color: Colors.white, size: 18),
          const SizedBox(width: 8),
          Text(
            label,
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white,
              fontSize: 12,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 1.2,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 74: quality_indicator.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\camera\widgets\quality_indicator.dart`
**Size:** 2.40 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

/// âœ… FEATURE 3 + 4: Quality Indicator Widget
class QualityIndicator extends StatelessWidget {
  final double blur;
  final double brightness;
  final String? warning;

  const QualityIndicator({
    super.key,
    required this.blur,
    required this.brightness,
    this.warning,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    if (warning == null) return const SizedBox.shrink();

    return Center(
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20, vertical: 12),
        margin: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: _getWarningColor().withOpacity(0.9),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          border: Border.all(color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.3), width: 1),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.3),
              blurRadius: 12,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(
              _getWarningIcon(),
              color: Colors.white,
              size: 20,
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 10),
            Flexible(
              child: Text(
                warning!,
                style: const TextStyle(
                  color: Colors.white,
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                ),
                textAlign: TextAlign.center,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Color _getWarningColor() {
    if (blur < 60) return const Color(0xFFE17055); // Red - Very blurry
    if (blur < 80) return const Color(0xFFFDCB6E); // Yellow - Slightly blurry
    if (brightness < 0.3) return const Color(0xFF6C5CE7); // Purple - Dark
    if (brightness > 0.85) return const Color(0xFFFDCB6E); // Yellow - Bright
    return const Color(0xFF00B894); // Green - Good
  }

  IconData _getWarningIcon() {
    if (warning!.contains('blur')) return Icons.blur_on;
    if (warning!.contains('light')) return Icons.lightbulb_outline;
    if (warning!.contains('bright')) return Icons.wb_sunny;
    if (warning!.contains('closer')) return Icons.zoom_in;
    return Icons.warning_amber_rounded;
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../models/scan_state.dart'; // âœ… Fixed

class CameraTopBar extends StatelessWidget {
  final CameraConfig config;
  final VoidCallback onClose;
  final VoidCallback onModeToggle;
  final VoidCallback onFlashToggle;

  const CameraTopBar({
    super.key,
    required this.config,
    required this.onClose,
    required this.onModeToggle,
    required this.onFlashToggle,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 12),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        gradient: LinearGradient(
          begin: Alignment.topCenter,
          end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
          colors: [
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.75),
            Colors.black.withOpacity(0.4),
            Colors.transparent,
          ],
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Row(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
          children: [
            _buildCloseButton(),
            _buildModeToggle(),
            _buildFlashButton(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCloseButton() {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onClose,
      child: Container(
        width: 44,
        height: 44,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1),
          shape: BoxShape.circle,
        ),
        child: const Icon(Icons.close, color: Colors.white, size: 24),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildModeToggle() {
    final isAutoMode = config.isAutoMode;
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onModeToggle,
      child: AnimatedContainer(
        duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 250),
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20, vertical: 10),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: isAutoMode
              ? AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.25)
              : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.12),
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(24),
          border: Border.all(
            color: isAutoMode
                ? AppColors.primary
                : Colors.white.withOpacity(0.25),
            width: 2,
          ),
        ),
        child: Row(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            if (isAutoMode)
              Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 8),
                child: Container(
                  width: 10,
                  height: 10,
                  decoration: BoxDecoration(
                    color: AppColors.primary,
                    shape: BoxShape.circle,
                    boxShadow: [
                      BoxShadow(
                        color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.6),
                        blurRadius: 6,
                        spreadRadius: 1,
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
              ),
            Text(
              config.modeText,
              style: TextStyle(
                color:
                isAutoMode ? AppColors.primaryLight : Colors.white,
                fontSize: 15,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                letterSpacing: 0.5,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFlashButton() {
    IconData icon;
    Color color;
    Color bgColor;

    switch (config.flashMode) {
      case CameraFlashMode.on:
        icon = Icons.flash_on;
        color = AppColors.primaryLight;
        bgColor = AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.2);
        break;
      case CameraFlashMode.auto:
        icon = Icons.flash_auto;
        color = const Color(0xFFFDCB6E);
        bgColor = const Color(0xFFFDCB6E).withOpacity(0.15);
        break;
      default:
        icon = Icons.flash_off;
        color = Colors.white;
        bgColor = Colors.white.withOpacity(0.1);
    }

    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onFlashToggle,
      child: Container(
        width: 44,
        height: 44,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: bgColor,
          shape: BoxShape.circle,
          border: config.flashMode != CameraFlashMode.off
              ? Border.all(color: color.withOpacity(0.3), width: 1.5)
              : null,
        ),
        child: Stack(
          alignment: Alignment.center,
          children: [
            Icon(icon, color: color, size: 24),
            if (config.flashMode == CameraFlashMode.auto)
              Positioned(
                bottom: 8,
                right: 8,
                child: Container(
                  padding: const EdgeInsets.all(2),
                  decoration: const BoxDecoration(
                    color: Colors.black,
                    shape: BoxShape.circle,
                  ),
                  child: const Text(
                    'A',
                    style: TextStyle(
                      color: Color(0xFFFDCB6E),
                      fontSize: 8,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                    ),
                  ),
                ),
              ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

/// Scan Preview Screen - Main Widget
class DocumentEditScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final String imagePath;
  final int pageNumber;

  const DocumentEditScreen({
    super.key,
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.pageNumber,
  });

  @override
  State<DocumentEditScreen> createState() => _DocumentEditScreenState();
}

class _DocumentEditScreenState extends State<DocumentEditScreen> {
  late DocumentEditController _controller;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _controller = DocumentEditController(
      imagePath: widget.imagePath,
      pageNumber: widget.pageNumber,
      onStateChange: () => setState(() {}),
    );
    _controller.initialize();
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return PopScope(
      canPop: !_controller.isProcessing,
      onPopInvokedWithResult: (didPop, result) { // âœ… FIXED: Line 62
        if (!didPop && _controller.isProcessing) {
          _controller.showError('Please wait, processing...');
        }
      },
      child: Scaffold(
        backgroundColor: Colors.black,
        body: Stack(
          children: [
            DocumentEditUI(
              controller: _controller,
              onBack: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
              onShare: _controller.handleShare,
            ),
            if (_controller.isProcessing || _controller.isDetecting)
              _buildOverlay(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOverlay() {
    return Container(
      color: Colors.black.withValues(alpha: 0.54), // âœ… FIXED: Line 134
      child: Center(
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            const CircularProgressIndicator(color: Color(0xFFFF6B35)),
            const SizedBox(height: 16),
            Text(
              _controller.isDetecting ? 'Detecting document...' : 'Processing...',
              style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.white, fontSize: 16),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
```

### File 77: document_edit_controller.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\document_edit\controllers\document_edit_controller.dart`
**Size:** 5.02 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
import '../../../models/edit_state.dart';
import '../../../services/edge_detector_service.dart';
import '../../../services/image_processor.dart';
import '../../camera/document_enhance_screen.dart';

/// Document Edit Controller - Manages state and operations
class DocumentEditController {
  final String imagePath;
  final int pageNumber;
  final VoidCallback onStateChange;

  DocumentEditState state;
  DocumentDetectionResult? detectionResult;
  bool isDetecting = false;
  bool isProcessing = false;
  BuildContext? context;

  DocumentEditController({
    required this.imagePath,
    required this.pageNumber,
    required this.onStateChange,
  }) : state = DocumentEditState(imagePath: imagePath);

  // Getters
  DocumentEditState get currentState => state;
  DocumentDetectionResult? get detection => detectionResult;
  bool get detecting => isDetecting;
  bool get processing => isProcessing;

  bool get canContinue {
    if (isProcessing || isDetecting) return false;
    if (detectionResult == null) return true;
    if (!detectionResult!.detected) return true;
    return true;
  }

  String get continueButtonText {
    if (isProcessing) return 'Processing...';
    if (isDetecting) return 'Detecting...';

    final result = detectionResult;
    if (result == null) return 'Continue';

    if (!result.detected) return 'Continue (No edges detected)';
    if (result.quality == ScanQuality.poor) return 'Continue (Low quality)';
    if (result.quality == ScanQuality.average) return 'Continue (Average quality)';

    return 'Continue';
  }

  void setContext(BuildContext context) => this.context = context;

  Future<void> initialize() async {
    await runDetection();
  }

  Future<void> runDetection() async {
    if (isDetecting) return;

    isDetecting = true;
    onStateChange();

    try {
      final edgeDetector = EdgeDetectorService();
      final result = await edgeDetector.detectEdges(imagePath);

      detectionResult = result;
      state = state.copyWith(
        corners: result.corners,
        cornersDetected: result.detected,
      );

      isDetecting = false;
      onStateChange();

      final warning = result.warning;
      if (warning != null && warning.isNotEmpty) {
        showWarning(warning);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      isDetecting = false;
      onStateChange();
      showError('Detection failed: $e');
    }
  }

  void rotateDocument() {
    state = state.copyWith(rotation: state.rotation + 90);
    onStateChange();
    HapticFeedback.lightImpact();
  }

  void cropDocument() {
    HapticFeedback.lightImpact();
    showInfo('Manual crop coming soon');
  }

  void adjustDocument() {
    HapticFeedback.lightImpact();
    showInfo('Manual adjust coming soon');
  }

  Future<void> handleContinue(BuildContext context) async {
    isProcessing = true;
    onStateChange();
    HapticFeedback.heavyImpact();

    try {
      final result = await ImageProcessor.processImageWithPerspective(
        imagePath: imagePath,
        corners: state.corners,
        enhanceText: true,
        removeShadow: true,
      );

      if (!result.success) {
        throw Exception(result.errorMessage ?? 'Processing failed');
      }

      if (context.mounted) {
        await Navigator.pushReplacement(
          context,
          MaterialPageRoute(
            builder: (_) => DocumentEnhanceScreen(
              imagePath: result.processedPath ?? imagePath,
              originalPath: imagePath,
              pageNumber: pageNumber,
              detectionResult: detectionResult!,
            ),
          ),
        );
      }
    } catch (e) {
      showError('Processing failed: $e');
    } finally {
      isProcessing = false;
      onStateChange();
    }
  }

  void handleShare() {
    showInfo('Share feature coming soon');
  }

  void showError(String message) {
    final context = this.context;
    if (context != null && context.mounted) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(
          content: Text(message),
          backgroundColor: Colors.red,
          behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  void showWarning(String message) {
    final context = this.context;
    if (context != null && context.mounted) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(
          content: Text(message),
          backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFFFB74D),
          behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  void showInfo(String message) {
    final context = this.context;
    if (context != null && context.mounted) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(
          content: Text(message),
          backgroundColor: Colors.blue,
          behavior: SnackBarBehavior.floating,
        ),
      );
    }
  }

  void dispose() {
    // Cleanup if needed
  }
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class CornerHandle extends StatefulWidget {
  final Offset position;
  final Function(Offset) onDrag;

  const CornerHandle({
    super.key,
    required this.position,
    required this.onDrag,
  });

  @override
  State<CornerHandle> createState() => _CornerHandleState();
}

class _CornerHandleState extends State<CornerHandle> {
  bool _isDragging = false;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Positioned(
      left: widget.position.dx - 12,
      top: widget.position.dy - 12,
      child: GestureDetector(
        onPanStart: (_) => setState(() => _isDragging = true),
        onPanUpdate: (details) {
          widget.onDrag(widget.position + details.delta);
        },
        onPanEnd: (_) => setState(() => _isDragging = false),
        child: AnimatedContainer(
          duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 150),
          width: _isDragging ? 32 : 24,
          height: _isDragging ? 32 : 24,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.primary,
            shape: BoxShape.circle,
            border: Border.all(
              color: Colors.white,
              width: _isDragging ? 3 : 2,
            ),
            boxShadow: [
              BoxShadow(
                color: AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: _isDragging ? 0.6 : 0.4),
                blurRadius: _isDragging ? 16 : 8,
                spreadRadius: _isDragging ? 2 : 0,
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

/// Shows document detection status with confidence
class DetectionStatusBanner extends StatelessWidget {
  final bool detected;
  final double confidence;
  final String? errorMessage;

  const DetectionStatusBanner({
    super.key,
    required this.detected,
    required this.confidence,
    this.errorMessage,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return AnimatedContainer(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 8),
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: _getBackgroundColor(),
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
        boxShadow: [
          BoxShadow(
            color: _getBackgroundColor().withValues(alpha: 0.4),
            blurRadius: 12,
            offset: const Offset(0, 4),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          Icon(
            _getIcon(),
            color: Colors.white,
            size: 18,
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 8),
          Text(
            _getMessage(),
            style: const TextStyle(
              color: Colors.white,
              fontSize: 12,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 1.2,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Color _getBackgroundColor() {
    if (detected) return AppColors.success;
    if (errorMessage != null) return AppColors.error;
    return AppColors.warning;
  }

  IconData _getIcon() {
    if (detected) return Icons.check_circle;
    if (errorMessage != null) return Icons.error;
    return Icons.warning_amber_rounded;
  }

  String _getMessage() {
    if (detected) return 'DOCUMENT DETECTED';
    if (errorMessage != null) return errorMessage!.toUpperCase();
    return 'ADJUST DOCUMENT';
  }
}
```

```dart
            },

          onCrop: controller.cropDocument,
          onAdjust: controller.adjustDocument,
          onReset: () => controller.runDetection(),

          onContinue: () => controller.handleContinue(context),
```

### File 82: document_preview.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\document_edit\widgets\document_preview.dart`
**Size:** 3.31 KB

```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../models/edit_state.dart';
import 'corner_handle.dart';
import 'detection_banner.dart';

class DocumentPreview extends StatelessWidget {
  final DocumentEditState state;
  final Function(int, Offset) onCornerDragged;

  const DocumentPreview({
    super.key,
    required this.state,
    required this.onCornerDragged,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
      child: Stack(
        children: [
          Center(child: _buildImage()),
          if (state.cornersDetected) _buildCornerOverlay(),
          Positioned(
            top: 16,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            child: DetectionBanner(detected: state.cornersDetected),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildImage() {
    return ClipRRect(
      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      child: Transform.rotate(
        angle: state.rotation * (3.14159 / 180),
        child: Image.file(
          File(state.imagePath),
          fit: BoxFit.contain,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCornerOverlay() {
    if (state.corners.length != 4) return const SizedBox.shrink();

    return CustomPaint(
      painter: EdgeLinePainter(corners: state.corners),
      child: Stack(
        children: List.generate(
          4,
              (index) => CornerHandle(
            position: state.corners[index],
            onDrag: (newPos) => onCornerDragged(index, newPos),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

/// Painter for dashed edge detection lines
class EdgeLinePainter extends CustomPainter {
  final List<Offset> corners;

  EdgeLinePainter({required this.corners});

  @override
  void paint(Canvas canvas, Size size) {
    if (corners.length != 4) return;

    final paint = Paint()
      ..color = Colors.white
      ..strokeWidth = 2
      ..style = PaintingStyle.stroke
      ..strokeCap = StrokeCap.round;

    // Draw dashed lines between corners
    _drawDashedLine(canvas, corners[0], corners[1], paint);
    _drawDashedLine(canvas, corners[1], corners[3], paint);
    _drawDashedLine(canvas, corners[3], corners[2], paint);
    _drawDashedLine(canvas, corners[2], corners[0], paint);
  }

  void _drawDashedLine(
      Canvas canvas,
      Offset start,
      Offset end,
      Paint paint,
      ) {
    const dashWidth = 8.0;
    const dashSpace = 4.0;
    final distance = (end - start).distance;
    final normalizedDx = (end.dx - start.dx) / distance;
    final normalizedDy = (end.dy - start.dy) / distance;

    var currentDistance = 0.0;
    while (currentDistance < distance) {
      final dashEnd = currentDistance + dashWidth;
      canvas.drawLine(
        Offset(
          start.dx + normalizedDx * currentDistance,
          start.dy + normalizedDy * currentDistance,
        ),
        Offset(
          start.dx + normalizedDx * (dashEnd > distance ? distance : dashEnd),
          start.dy + normalizedDy * (dashEnd > distance ? distance : dashEnd),
        ),
        paint,
      );
      currentDistance += dashWidth + dashSpace;
    }
  }

  @override
  bool shouldRepaint(EdgeLinePainter oldDelegate) =>
      corners != oldDelegate.corners;
}

```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';

class EditActionButtons extends StatelessWidget {

  final VoidCallback onContinue;
  final bool isProcessing;
  final bool canContinue;

  const EditActionButtons({
    super.key,
    required this.onRetake,
    required this.onContinue,
    this.isProcessing = false,
    this.canContinue = true,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(width: 16),

            child: _FilledButton(
              label: 'Continue',
              onTap: (canContinue && !isProcessing) ? onContinue : null,
              isProcessing: isProcessing,

          ),

      ),
    );

class _OutlinedButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final String label;
  final VoidCallback? onTap;

  const _OutlinedButton({required this.label, this.onTap});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Opacity(
      opacity: onTap == null ? 0.5 : 1.0,
      child: GestureDetector(
        onTap: onTap,
        child: Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
            border: Border.all(color: AppColors.primary, width: 2),
          ),
          child: Center(
            child: Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: AppColors.primary,
                fontSize: 16,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _FilledButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final String label;
  final VoidCallback? onTap;
  final bool isProcessing;

  const _FilledButton({
    required this.label,
    this.onTap,
    this.isProcessing = false,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Opacity(
      opacity: onTap == null ? 0.5 : 1.0,
      child: GestureDetector(
        onTap: onTap,
        child: Container(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 16),
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            gradient: const LinearGradient(
              colors: [Color(0xFFFF6933), Color(0xFFFF8C61)],
            ),
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
          ),
          child: Center(
            child: isProcessing
                ? const SizedBox(
              width: 20,
              height: 20,
              child: CircularProgressIndicator(
                color: Colors.white,
                strokeWidth: 2,
              ),
            )
                : Text(
              label,
              style: const TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 16,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ),

    );
```

```dart
class _ActionButton extends StatelessWidget {
  final IconData icon;
  final String label;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const _ActionButton({
    required this.icon,
    required this.label,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

            icon,
```

### File 86: filter_selector.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\document_edit\widgets\filter_selector.dart`
**Size:** 3.63 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../models/edit_state.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class FilterSelector extends StatelessWidget {
  final DocumentFilter selectedFilter;
  final Function(DocumentFilter) onFilterSelected;

  const FilterSelector({
    super.key,
    required this.selectedFilter,
    required this.onFilterSelected,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.center,
      children: [
        const Padding(
          padding: EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(16, 24, 16, 16),
          child: Text(
            'FILTERS',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 11,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              letterSpacing: 2.0,
              color: Color(0xFFCE9E8D), // Dark theme text color
            ),
          ),
        ),
        SizedBox(
          height: 100,
          child: ListView.builder(
            scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
            padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16),
            itemCount: DocumentFilter.values.length,
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              final filter = DocumentFilter.values[index];
              final isSelected = filter == selectedFilter;

              return Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 24),
                child: _FilterChip(
                  filter: filter,
                  isSelected: isSelected,
                  onTap: () => onFilterSelected(filter),
                ),
              );
            },
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

class _FilterChip extends StatelessWidget {
  final DocumentFilter filter;
  final bool isSelected;
  final VoidCallback onTap;

  const _FilterChip({
    required this.filter,
    required this.isSelected,
    required this.onTap,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Column(
        mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
        children: [
          // Filter thumbnail
          AnimatedContainer(
            duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 200),
            width: 56,
            height: 56,
            decoration: BoxDecoration(
              color: const Color(0xFF2C2C2C),
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              border: Border.all(
                color: isSelected ? AppColors.primary : Colors.transparent,
                width: isSelected ? 2 : 0,
              ),
              boxShadow: isSelected
                  ? [
                BoxShadow(
                  color: AppColors.primary.withValues(alpha: 0.2),
                  blurRadius: 8,
                  spreadRadius: 2,
                ),
              ]
                  : null,
            ),
            child: ClipRRect(
              borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(10),
              child: Icon(
                Icons.image,
                color: isSelected
                    ? AppColors.primary
                    : Colors.grey.shade600,
                size: 28,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          // Filter label
          Text(
            filter.displayName,
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 11,
              fontWeight: isSelected ? FontWeight.bold : FontWeight.w500,
              color: isSelected
                  ? AppColors.primary
                  : const Color(0xFFCE9E8D),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'widgets/greeting_card.dart';
import 'widgets/scan_button.dart';
import 'widgets/quick_actions.dart';
import 'widgets/smart_tools.dart';
import 'widgets/recent_files.dart';
import 'widgets/bottom_nav.dart';

class HomeScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const HomeScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<HomeScreen> createState() => _HomeScreenState();
}

class _HomeScreenState extends State<HomeScreen> {
  int _selectedIndex = 0;

  void _onNavItemTapped(int index) {
    setState(() {
      _selectedIndex = index;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          _buildBackgroundGradients(),
          _buildContent(),
        ],
      ),
      bottomNavigationBar: BottomNav(
        selectedIndex: _selectedIndex,
        onItemTapped: _onNavItemTapped,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBackgroundGradients() {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Positioned(
          top: -150,
          left: -80,
          child: _buildGradientCircle(320, 0.05),
        ),
        Positioned(
          top: MediaQuery.of(context).size.height * 0.4,
          right: -40,
          child: _buildGradientCircle(256, 0.08),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildGradientCircle(double size, double opacity) {
    return Container(
      width: size,
      height: size,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        shape: BoxShape.circle,
        gradient: RadialGradient(
          colors: [
            Theme.of(context).primaryColor.withOpacity(opacity),
            Colors.transparent,
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildContent() {
    return SafeArea(
      child: Column(
        children: [
          _buildAppBar(),
          Expanded(
            child: SingleChildScrollView(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24.0),
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: const [
                  GreetingCard(),
                  SizedBox(height: 24),
                  ScanButton(),
                  SizedBox(height: 32),
                  QuickActions(),
                  SizedBox(height: 32),
                  SmartTools(),
                  SizedBox(height: 32),
                  RecentFiles(),
                  SizedBox(height: 100),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAppBar() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 16),
      child: Row(
        mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
        children: [
          _buildAppLogo(),
          _buildAppBarActions(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAppLogo() {
    return Row(
      children: [
        Container(
          width: 32,
          height: 32,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: Theme.of(context).primaryColor,
            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
            boxShadow: [
              BoxShadow(
                color: Theme.of(context).primaryColor.withOpacity(0.2),
                blurRadius: 8,
                offset: const Offset(0, 2),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          child: const Center(
            child: Text(
              'IQ',
              style: TextStyle(
                color: Colors.white,
                fontSize: 12,
                fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(width: 8),
        const Text(
          'ScanIQ',
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 20,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
            letterSpacing: -0.5,
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAppBarActions() {
    return Row(
      children: [
        IconButton(
          icon: const Icon(Icons.search),
          onPressed: () {
            // TODO: Implement search
          },
        ),
        IconButton(
          icon: const Icon(Icons.menu),
          onPressed: () {
            _showMenu();
          },
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  void _showMenu() {
    showModalBottomSheet(
      context: context,
      shape: const RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(20)),
      ),
      builder: (context) => Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.person, 'My Account'),
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.settings, 'Settings'),
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.workspace_premium, 'Upgrade to Pro'),
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.help, 'Help & Support'),
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.privacy_tip, 'Privacy Policy'),
            _buildMenuItem(Icons.info, 'About'),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildMenuItem(IconData icon, String title) {
    return ListTile(
      leading: Icon(icon, color: Theme.of(context).primaryColor),
      title: Text(title),
      onTap: () {
        Navigator.pop(context);
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(content: Text('$title tapped')),
        );
      },
    );
  }
}
```

### File 88: bottom_nav.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\home\widgets\bottom_nav.dart`
**Size:** 3.04 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../services/camera_service.dart';

class BottomNav extends StatelessWidget {
  final int selectedIndex;
  final Function(int) onItemTapped;

  const BottomNav({
    super.key,
    required this.selectedIndex,
    required this.onItemTapped,
  });

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Container(
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.9),
        border: Border(
          top: BorderSide(color: Colors.grey.shade100, width: 1),
        ),
      ),
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 24, vertical: 8),
          child: Row(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
            children: [
              _buildNavItem(context, 0, Icons.home, 'Home', true),
              _buildNavItem(context, 1, Icons.folder, 'Files', false),
              _buildCenterButton(context),
              _buildNavItem(context, 2, Icons.share, 'Shared', false),
              _buildNavItem(context, 3, Icons.settings, 'Settings', false),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildNavItem(
      BuildContext context,
      int index,
      IconData icon,
      String label,
      bool filled,
      ) {
    final isSelected = selectedIndex == index;

    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: () => onItemTapped(index),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Icon(
              icon,
              color: isSelected ? AppColors.primary : Colors.grey.shade400,
              size: 24,
              fill: (isSelected && filled) ? 1.0 : 0.0,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 4),
            Text(
              label,
              style: TextStyle(
                fontSize: 10,
                fontWeight: isSelected ? FontWeight.bold : FontWeight.w500,
                color: isSelected ? AppColors.primary : Colors.grey.shade400,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildCenterButton(BuildContext context) {
    return Transform.translate(
      offset: const Offset(0, -10),
      child: GestureDetector(
        onTap: () => CameraService.scanDocument(context),
        child: Container(
          width: 56,
          height: 56,
          decoration: BoxDecoration(
            color: AppColors.primary,
            shape: BoxShape.circle,
            boxShadow: [
              BoxShadow(
                color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.3),
                blurRadius: 15,
                offset: const Offset(0, 5),
              ),
            ],
          ),
          child: const Icon(
            Icons.add,
            color: Colors.white,
            size: 28,
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
```

```dart
class QuickActions extends StatelessWidget {

  Widget build(BuildContext context) {

      shrinkWrap: true,

      mainAxisSpacing: 16,
      childAspectRatio: 1.4,
      children: [
        _buildActionCard(
          context,
          icon: Icons.picture_as_pdf,
          title: 'Scan PDF',
          onTap: () => CameraService.scanPDF(context),
        ),
        _buildActionCard(
          context,
          icon: Icons.text_fields,
          title: 'Extract Text',
          onTap: () => _showFeature(context, 'Extract Text'),
        ),
        _buildActionCard(
          context,
          icon: Icons.upload_file,
          title: 'Import',
          onTap: () => _showFeature(context, 'Import Files'),
        ),
        _buildActionCard(
          context,
          icon: Icons.psychology,
          title: 'AI Assistant',
          onTap: () => _showFeature(context, 'AI Assistant'),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionCard(
      BuildContext context, {
        required IconData icon,
        required String title,
        required VoidCallback onTap,
      }) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey.shade100),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.03),
              blurRadius: 20,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            Container(
              width: 40,
              height: 40,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.1),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
              ),
              child: Icon(
                icon,
                color: AppColors.primary,
                size: 22,
              ),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 10),
            Flexible(
              child: Text(
                title,
                style: const TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                ),
                maxLines: 1,
                overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showFeature(BuildContext context, String feature) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(
        content: Text('$feature will open here'),
        duration: const Duration(seconds: 2),
        backgroundColor: AppColors.primary,
      ),
    );
```

### File 91: recent_files.dart

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';
import '../../../services/file_service.dart';
import '../../../models/document_model.dart';

class RecentFiles extends StatelessWidget {
  const RecentFiles({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    final files = FileService.getRecentFiles();

    return Column(
      crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
      children: [
        const Text(
          'Recent Files',
          style: TextStyle(
            fontSize: 18,
            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(height: 16),
        if (files.isEmpty)
          _buildEmptyState()
        else
          ListView.separated(
            shrinkWrap: true,
            physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
            itemCount: files.length,
            separatorBuilder: (context, index) => const SizedBox(height: 12),
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              return _buildFileCard(context, files[index]);
            },
          ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFileCard(BuildContext context, DocumentModel doc) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: () => _openFile(context, doc),
      child: Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(12),
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: Colors.white,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(16),
          border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey.shade100),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0.03),
              blurRadius: 20,
              offset: const Offset(0, 4),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            _buildThumbnail(doc.type),
            const SizedBox(width: 16),
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    doc.name,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 14,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
                    ),
                    maxLines: 1,
                    overflow: TextOverflow.ellipsis,
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 4),
                  Text(
                    '${doc.formattedDate} â€¢ ${doc.formattedSize}',
                    style: TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 12,
                      color: Colors.grey.shade500,
                    ),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
            IconButton(
              icon: const Icon(Icons.more_vert),
              color: Colors.grey.shade400,
              onPressed: () => _showFileOptions(context, doc),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildThumbnail(DocumentType type) {
    return Container(
      width: 64,
      height: 64,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        color: Colors.grey.shade100,
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
      ),
      child: Icon(
        type == DocumentType.pdf ? Icons.picture_as_pdf : Icons.image,
        color: Colors.grey.shade300,
        size: 32,
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildEmptyState() {
    return Container(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.all(32),
      child: Column(
        children: [
          Icon(
            Icons.folder_open,
            size: 64,
            color: Colors.grey.shade300,
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 16),
          Text(
            'No documents yet',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 16,
              fontWeight: FontWeight.w600,
              color: Colors.grey.shade600,
            ),
          ),
          const SizedBox(height: 8),
          Text(
            'Tap the scan button to get started',
            style: TextStyle(
              fontSize: 14,
              color: Colors.grey.shade500,
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  void _openFile(BuildContext context, DocumentModel doc) {
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
      SnackBar(content: Text('Opening ${doc.name}')),
    );
  }

  void _showFileOptions(BuildContext context, DocumentModel doc) {
    showModalBottomSheet(
      context: context,
      shape: const RoundedRectangleBorder(
        borderRadius: BorderRadius.vertical(top: Radius.circular(20)),
      ),
      builder: (context) => Container(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
        child: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            _buildOption(context, Icons.share, 'Share', () {
              Navigator.pop(context);
              FileService.shareFile(doc.id);
            }),
            _buildOption(context, Icons.edit, 'Rename', () {
              Navigator.pop(context);
            }),
            _buildOption(context, Icons.delete, 'Delete', () {
              Navigator.pop(context);
              FileService.deleteFile(doc.id);
            }),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildOption(
      BuildContext context,
      IconData icon,
      String title,
      VoidCallback onTap,
      ) {
    return ListTile(
      leading: Icon(icon, color: AppColors.primary),
      title: Text(title),
      onTap: onTap,
    );
  }
}
```

### File 95: splash_screen.dart
**Path:** `lib\screens\splash\splash_screen.dart`
**Size:** 3.34 KB

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'dart:async';
import '../../core/routes/app_routes.dart';
import 'widgets/app_logo.dart';
import 'widgets/brand_text.dart';
import 'widgets/loading_indicator.dart';

class SplashScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const SplashScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<SplashScreen> createState() => _SplashScreenState();
}

class _SplashScreenState extends State<SplashScreen>
    with SingleTickerProviderStateMixin {
  late AnimationController _controller;
  late Animation<double> _fadeAnimation;
  double _progress = 0.0;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    _setupAnimation();
    _startProgress();
  }

  void _setupAnimation() {
    _controller = AnimationController(
      duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 1500),
      vsync: this,
    );

    _fadeAnimation = Tween<double>(begin: 0.0, end: 1.0).animate(
      CurvedAnimation(parent: _controller, curve: Curves.easeIn),
    );

    _controller.forward();
  }

  void _startProgress() {
    Timer.periodic(const Duration(milliseconds: 30), (timer) {
      if (mounted) {
        setState(() {
          _progress += 0.02;
          if (_progress >= 1.0) {
            _progress = 1.0;
            timer.cancel();
            _navigateToHome();
          }
        });
      }
    });
  }

  void _navigateToHome() {
    Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500), () {
      if (mounted) {
        AppRoutes.navigateToHome(context);
      }
    });
  }

  @override
  void dispose() {
    _controller.dispose();
    super.dispose();
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Stack(
        children: [
          _buildBackgroundGradients(),
          _buildContent(),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildBackgroundGradients() {
    return Stack(
      children: [
        Positioned(
          top: -100,
          left: -100,
          child: _buildGradientCircle(250, 0.05),
        ),
        Positioned(
          bottom: -50,
          right: -50,
          child: _buildGradientCircle(300, 0.08),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildGradientCircle(double size, double opacity) {
    return Container(
      width: size,
      height: size,
      decoration: BoxDecoration(
        shape: BoxShape.circle,
        gradient: RadialGradient(
          colors: [
            Theme.of(context).primaryColor.withOpacity(opacity),
            Colors.transparent,
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildContent() {
    return FadeTransition(
      opacity: _fadeAnimation,
      child: SafeArea(
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
            horizontal: 24.0,
            vertical: 48.0,
          ),
          child: Column(
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
            children: [
              const SizedBox(height: 20),
              const Column(
                mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
                children: [
                  AppLogo(),
                  SizedBox(height: 32),
                  BrandText(),
                ],
              ),
              LoadingIndicator(progress: _progress),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_strings.dart';
import '../../../core/constants/app_colors.dart';

class AppLogo extends StatelessWidget {
  const AppLogo({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Hero(
      tag: 'app_logo',
      child: Container(
        width: 120,
        height: 140,
        decoration: BoxDecoration(
          color: AppColors.primary,
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
          boxShadow: [
            BoxShadow(
              color: AppColors.primary.withOpacity(0.3),
              blurRadius: 20,
              offset: const Offset(0, 10),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        child: Stack(
          children: [
            _buildFoldedCorner(),
            _buildLogoText(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildFoldedCorner() {
    return Positioned(
      top: 0,
      right: 0,
      child: CustomPaint(
        size: const Size(40, 40),
        painter: _FoldedCornerPainter(),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildLogoText() {
    return const Center(
      child: Text(
        AppStrings.logoText,
        style: TextStyle(
          fontSize: 48,
          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
          color: Colors.white,
          letterSpacing: -2,
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class _FoldedCornerPainter extends CustomPainter {
  @override
  void paint(Canvas canvas, Size size) {
    final paint = Paint()
      ..color = Colors.white.withOpacity(0.2)
      ..style = PaintingStyle.fill;

    final path = Path()
      ..moveTo(size.width, 0)
      ..lineTo(size.width, size.height)
      ..lineTo(0, size.height)
      ..close();

    canvas.drawPath(path, paint);
  }

  @override
  bool shouldRepaint(covariant CustomPainter oldDelegate) => false;
}
```

### File 99: background_processor.dart

```dart
import 'dart:isolate';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';

/// âœ… Background image processing (prevents UI freeze)
class BackgroundProcessor {
  static Future<T> compute<T>(
      Future<T> Function() task, {
        String? debugLabel,
      }) async {
    if (kDebugMode && debugLabel != null) {
      debugPrint('ğŸ”„ Background task started: $debugLabel');
    }

    try {
      final result = await Isolate.run(task);

      if (kDebugMode && debugLabel != null) {
        debugPrint('âœ… Background task completed: $debugLabel');
      }

      return result;
    } catch (e) {
      if (kDebugMode) {
        debugPrint('âŒ Background task failed: $e');
      }
      rethrow;
    }
  }
}

/// âœ… Detection task (runs in isolate)
class DetectionTask {
  static Future<Map<String, dynamic>> detectEdges(String imagePath) async {
    return BackgroundProcessor.compute(
          () async {
        // Your edge detection logic here
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(milliseconds: 500));

        return {
          'detected': true,
          'corners': [],
          'confidence': 0.85,
        };
      },
      debugLabel: 'Edge Detection',
    );
  }
}

/// âœ… Processing task (runs in isolate)
class ProcessingTask {
  static Future<String> processImage({
    required String imagePath,
    required List corners,
  }) async {
    return BackgroundProcessor.compute(
          () async {
        // Your image processing logic here
        await Future.delayed(const Duration(seconds: 1));

        return imagePath; // Return processed path
      },
      debugLabel: 'Image Processing',
    );
  }
}
```

```dart
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:image_picker/image_picker.dart';
import '../screens/camera/camera_screen_v2.dart';

class CameraService {
  static final ImagePicker _picker = ImagePicker();

  static Future<void> scanDocument(BuildContext context) async {
    if (!await _requestCameraPermission()) {
      if (context.mounted) {
        _showPermissionDialog(context);
      }
      return;
    }

    if (context.mounted) {
      Navigator.push(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const CameraScreenV2()),
      );
    }
  }

  static Future<bool> _requestCameraPermission() async {
    // Camera permission logic
    return true;
  }

  static void _showPermissionDialog(BuildContext context) {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text('Camera Permission'),
        content: const Text('Camera permission is required to scan documents.'),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            child: const Text('OK'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}
```

### File 101: document_detector.dart
**Path:** `lib\services\document_detector.dart`
**Size:** 9.97 KB

```dart
import 'dart:async';
import 'package:camera/camera.dart';
import 'package:flutter/foundation.dart';
import '../models/scan_state.dart'; // âœ… FIXED: scan_state.dart (with underscore)

class DocumentDetector {
  // Thresholds
  static const double minConfidence = 0.75;
  static const double highConfidence = 0.85;
  static const int stabilityFrames = 3; // Reduced for faster response
  static const double blurThreshold = 100.0; // Laplacian variance threshold
  static const double minDocumentArea = 0.20; // 20% of frame
  static const double maxDocumentArea = 0.95; // 95% of frame
  static const double angleThreshold = 15.0; // degrees

  // State tracking
  final List<double> _recentConfidences = [];
  final List<double> _recentBrightness = [];
  final List<bool> _recentBlurStatus = [];
  DateTime? _lastDetectionTime;
  int _stableFrameCount = 0;

  /// Analyzes camera frame for document detection
  DocumentDetectionResult analyzeFrame(CameraImage? image) {
    if (image == null) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult.notDetected();
    }

    // Step 1: Brightness check
    final brightness = _estimateBrightness(image);
    _recentBrightness.add(brightness);
    if (_recentBrightness.length > stabilityFrames) {
      _recentBrightness.removeAt(0);
    }

    if (brightness < 0.25) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.idle,
        confidence: 0.0,
        isDetected: false,
        warning: DetectionWarning.lowLight,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: 0.0,
        rotationAngle: 0.0,
      );
    }

    if (brightness > 0.85) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.idle,
        confidence: 0.0,
        isDetected: false,
        warning: DetectionWarning.glare,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: 0.0,
        rotationAngle: 0.0,
      );
    }

    // Step 2: Blur detection (simulated via brightness variance)
    final blurScore = _detectBlur(image);
    final isBlurry = blurScore < blurThreshold;
    _recentBlurStatus.add(isBlurry);
    if (_recentBlurStatus.length > stabilityFrames) {
      _recentBlurStatus.removeAt(0);
    }

    if (isBlurry) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.blur,
        confidence: 0.0,
        isDetected: false,
        warning: DetectionWarning.blur,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: blurScore,
        rotationAngle: 0.0,
      );
    }

    // Step 3: Edge detection simulation
    final edgeResult = _simulateEdgeDetection(brightness, image);
    final confidence = edgeResult['confidence'] as double;
    final area = edgeResult['area'] as double;
    final angle = edgeResult['angle'] as double;

    _recentConfidences.add(confidence);
    if (_recentConfidences.length > stabilityFrames) {
      _recentConfidences.removeAt(0);
    }

    // Step 4: Check document size
    if (area < minDocumentArea) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.tooSmall,
        confidence: confidence,
        isDetected: false,
        warning: DetectionWarning.tooFar,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: blurScore,
        rotationAngle: angle,
      );
    }

    // Step 5: Check tilt
    if (angle > angleThreshold) {
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.tilted,
        confidence: confidence,
        isDetected: true,
        warning: DetectionWarning.tilted,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: blurScore,
        rotationAngle: angle,
      );
    }

    // Step 6: Check stability
    final isStable = _isStable();

    if (confidence >= minConfidence && confidence < highConfidence) {
      if (!isStable) {
        return DocumentDetectionResult(
          state: ScanState.detecting,
          confidence: confidence,
          isDetected: true,
          warning: DetectionWarning.unstable,
          brightness: brightness,
          blurScore: blurScore,
          rotationAngle: angle,
        );
      }
      return DocumentDetectionResult(
        state: ScanState.detecting,
        confidence: confidence,
        isDetected: true,
        warning: null,
        brightness: brightness,
        blurScore: blurScore,
        rotationAngle: angle,
      );
    }

    // Step 7: Ready to capture
    if (confidence >= highConfidence && isStable) {
      _stableFrameCount++;
      if (_stableFrameCount >= stabilityFrames) {
        _lastDetectionTime ??= DateTime.now();
        return DocumentDetectionResult(
          state: ScanState.ready,
          confidence: confidence,
          isDetected: true,
          warning: null,
          brightness: brightness,
          blurScore: blurScore,
          rotationAngle: angle,
        );
      }
    } else {
      _stableFrameCount = 0;
    }

    return DocumentDetectionResult(
      state: ScanState.detecting,
      confidence: confidence,
      isDetected: true,
      warning: null,
      brightness: brightness,
      blurScore: blurScore,
      rotationAngle: angle,
    );
  }

  /// Estimates brightness from camera image
  double _estimateBrightness(CameraImage image) {
    // Simulated: Analyze Y plane (luminance) from YUV format
    try {
      final plane = image.planes.first;
      final bytes = plane.bytes;

      // Sample every 10th pixel for performance
      int sum = 0;
      int count = 0;
      for (int i = 0; i < bytes.length; i += 10) {
        sum += bytes[i];
        count++;
      }

      final avgBrightness = sum / count / 255.0;
      return avgBrightness;
    } catch (e) {
      return 0.5; // Default
    }
  }

  /// Detects blur using Laplacian variance (simulated)
  double _detectBlur(CameraImage image) {
    // Real implementation would use Laplacian operator
    // For now, simulate based on brightness variance
    try {
      final plane = image.planes.first;
      final bytes = plane.bytes;

      // Calculate variance as blur indicator
      double sum = 0;
      double sumSq = 0;
      int count = 0;

      for (int i = 0; i < bytes.length; i += 5) {
        final val = bytes[i].toDouble();
        sum += val;
        sumSq += val * val;
        count++;
      }

      final mean = sum / count;
      final variance = (sumSq / count) - (mean * mean);

      return variance; // Higher = sharper
    } catch (e) {
      return 150.0; // Default
    }
  }

  /// Simulates edge detection and returns confidence, area, angle
  Map<String, double> _simulateEdgeDetection(double brightness, CameraImage image) {
    // Real implementation would use:
    // 1. Grayscale conversion
    // 2. Gaussian blur
    // 3. Canny edge detection
    // 4. Contour detection (find largest 4-point polygon)
    // 5. Perspective calculation

    // For now, simulate based on brightness and randomness
    double baseConfidence = 0.5;

    // Better confidence in good lighting
    if (brightness > 0.4 && brightness < 0.7) {
      baseConfidence = 0.85 + (DateTime.now().millisecond % 10) / 100;
    } else if (brightness >= 0.3 && brightness <= 0.8) {
      baseConfidence = 0.70 + (DateTime.now().millisecond % 15) / 100;
    } else {
      baseConfidence = 0.45 + (DateTime.now().millisecond % 20) / 100;
    }

    // Simulate document area (percentage of frame)
    final area = 0.35 + (DateTime.now().millisecond % 30) / 100;

    // Simulate rotation angle
    final angle = (DateTime.now().millisecond % 25).toDouble();

    return {
      'confidence': baseConfidence.clamp(0.0, 1.0),
      'area': area.clamp(0.0, 1.0),
      'angle': angle,
    };
  }

  /// Checks if detection is stable across recent frames
  bool _isStable() {
    if (_recentConfidences.length < stabilityFrames) {
      return false;
    }

    final avg = _recentConfidences.reduce((a, b) => a + b) / _recentConfidences.length;
    final variance = _recentConfidences
        .map((c) => (c - avg).abs())
        .reduce((a, b) => a + b);

    return variance < 0.10; // Threshold for stability
  }

  /// Resets detector state
  void reset() {
    _recentConfidences.clear();
    _recentBrightness.clear();
    _recentBlurStatus.clear();
    _lastDetectionTime = null;
    _stableFrameCount = 0;
  }
}

/// Detection warnings
enum DetectionWarning {
  lowLight,
  glare,
  tooFar,
  unstable,
  tilted,
  blur,
}

/// Document detection result
class DocumentDetectionResult {
  final ScanState state;
  final double confidence;
  final bool isDetected;
  final DetectionWarning? warning;
  final double brightness;
  final double blurScore;
  final double rotationAngle;

  DocumentDetectionResult({
    required this.state,
    required this.confidence,
    required this.isDetected,
    this.warning,
    required this.brightness,
    required this.blurScore,
    required this.rotationAngle,
  });

  factory DocumentDetectionResult.notDetected() {
    return DocumentDetectionResult(
      state: ScanState.idle,
      confidence: 0.0,
      isDetected: false,
      brightness: 0.0,
      blurScore: 0.0,
      rotationAngle: 0.0,
    );
  }

  /// Warning message for UI
  String get warningMessage {
    switch (warning) {
      case DetectionWarning.lowLight:
        return 'ğŸ’¡ Too dark - Turn on flash';
      case DetectionWarning.glare:
        return 'âœ¨ Too bright - Reduce glare';
      case DetectionWarning.tooFar:
        return 'ğŸ“ Move closer to document';
      case DetectionWarning.unstable:
        return 'ğŸ¤š Hold steady';
      case DetectionWarning.tilted:
        return 'ğŸ“ Straighten the document';
      case DetectionWarning.blur:
        return 'ğŸ” Hold steady - Blurry';
      default:
        return '';
    }
  }

  /// Should auto-capture?
  bool get shouldAutoCapture {
    return state == ScanState.ready &&
        confidence >= 0.85 &&
        warning == null &&
        blurScore >= 100.0 &&
        rotationAngle < 10.0;
  }
}

```

```dart
import '../models/document_model.dart';

class FileService {
  // Static list to store scanned documents (temporary in-memory storage)
  static final List<DocumentModel> _documents = [];

  /// Get all recent files (empty by default until user scans)
  static List<DocumentModel> getRecentFiles() {
    // Return actual scanned documents only
    // Initially empty, will be populated when user scans documents
    return List.from(_documents);
  }

  /// Add new scanned document
  static void addDocument(DocumentModel document) {
    _documents.insert(0, document); // Add to beginning (most recent first)
  }

  /// Delete a file by ID
  static Future<void> deleteFile(String id) async {
    _documents.removeWhere((doc) => doc.id == id);
    // TODO: Delete from actual storage
  }

  /// Share a file by ID
  static Future<void> shareFile(String id) async {
    // TODO: Implement file sharing functionality
  }

  /// Clear all documents (for testing)
  static void clearAll() {
    _documents.clear();
  }

  /// Get document by ID
  static DocumentModel? getDocumentById(String id) {
    try {
      return _documents.firstWhere((doc) => doc.id == id);
    } catch (e) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  /// Get total document count
  static int getDocumentCount() {
    return _documents.length;
  }
}
```

```text
# Project-level configuration.
cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.13)
project(runner LANGUAGES CXX)

# The name of the executable created for the application. Change this to change
# the on-disk name of your application.
set(BINARY_NAME "scaniq")
# The unique GTK application identifier for this application. See:
# https://wiki.gnome.org/HowDoI/ChooseApplicationID
set(APPLICATION_ID "com.scaniq.scaniq")

# Explicitly opt in to modern CMake behaviors to avoid warnings with recent
# versions of CMake.
cmake_policy(SET CMP0063 NEW)

# Load bundled libraries from the lib/ directory relative to the binary.
set(CMAKE_INSTALL_RPATH "$ORIGIN/lib")

# Root filesystem for cross-building.
if(FLUTTER_TARGET_PLATFORM_SYSROOT)
  set(CMAKE_SYSROOT ${FLUTTER_TARGET_PLATFORM_SYSROOT})
  set(CMAKE_FIND_ROOT_PATH ${CMAKE_SYSROOT})
  set(CMAKE_FIND_ROOT_PATH_MODE_PROGRAM NEVER)
  set(CMAKE_FIND_ROOT_PATH_MODE_PACKAGE ONLY)

  set(CMAKE_FIND_ROOT_PATH_MODE_INCLUDE ONLY)

  set(CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE "Debug" CACHE
    STRING "Flutter build mode" FORCE)
  set_property(CACHE CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE PROPERTY STRINGS
    "Debug" "Profile" "Release")
endif()

# Compilation settings that should be applied to most targets.
#
# Be cautious about adding new options here, as plugins use this function by
# default. In most cases, you should add new options to specific targets instead
# of modifying this function.
function(APPLY_STANDARD_SETTINGS TARGET)
  target_compile_features(${TARGET} PUBLIC cxx_std_14)
  target_compile_options(${TARGET} PRIVATE -Wall -Werror)
  target_compile_options(${TARGET} PRIVATE "$<$<NOT:$<CONFIG:Debug>>:-O3>")
  target_compile_definitions(${TARGET} PRIVATE "$<$<NOT:$<CONFIG:Debug>>:NDEBUG>")
endfunction()

# Flutter library and tool build rules.

add_subdirectory(${FLUTTER_MANAGED_DIR})

# System-level dependencies.
find_package(PkgConfig REQUIRED)
pkg_check_modules(GTK REQUIRED IMPORTED_TARGET gtk+-3.0)

# Application build; see runner/CMakeLists.txt.
add_subdirectory("runner")

# Run the Flutter tool portions of the build. This must not be removed.
add_dependencies(${BINARY_NAME} flutter_assemble)

# Only the install-generated bundle's copy of the executable will launch
# correctly, since the resources must in the right relative locations. To avoid
# people trying to run the unbundled copy, put it in a subdirectory instead of
# the default top-level location.
set_target_properties(${BINARY_NAME}
  PROPERTIES
  RUNTIME_OUTPUT_DIRECTORY "${CMAKE_BINARY_DIR}/intermediates_do_not_run"
)

# directory.
```
